British Foreign Secretary Hoare Announces Policy Towards China to the House of Commons: Close Attention Paid to Economic Conditions, Political Stability Shows Steady Progress, Hebei Issue Being Discussed by Telegram.

The newly appointed Foreign Secretary Hoare gave a highly anticipated speech on the overall situation in China in the House of Commons today, saying that the impact of the world's economic misfortunes on China has been later than expected for various reasons. In recent months, China's economic situation has been indeed difficult, and its position has become even more chaotic due to the recent rise in silver prices. The government is closely and sympathetically paying attention to all developments. The House of Commons knows that it is now planned to send Sir Ross, the chief of the British government's economic advisors, to China as soon as possible so that he can contribute opinions to London on the country's current economic situation. Although China's finances have encountered difficulties in recent months, its political situation has not deteriorated, and there is a steady trend towards order and consolidation. The central government's suppression of the communists also has the appearance of expanding its authority and power. However, in the past two weeks, there have been disturbing developments in North China. The various details that have been reported are contradictory, and the situation is in danger of rapid change. Japanese military authorities have made demands on the Chinese authorities because Chinese people and groups have engaged in anti-Japanese activities within the demilitarized zone delineated by the Tanggu Truce Agreement. The Chinese authorities have taken steps to meet these demands, but some points remain unresolved and will be discussed locally. As for the recent developments in North China, he has been discussing them by telegram with the British representatives stationed in Tokyo and Nanjing, and the two representatives are contacting the governments of their respective host countries. This telegram discussion is still in progress. (17th, Reuters Telegram)

The Scourge of Opium in North China: On-the-Spot Inspection by British Social Reformer: Who Is Making the Will of the Chinese People Decline?

Miss Muriel Lester, a British social reformer, recently investigated the opium trade in the demilitarized zone of North China and exposed many things. A special correspondent from the Manchester Guardian in Beiping wrote an article to elaborate on this, which was published by the newspaper along with an editorial saying, "Japan bears a major responsibility for this." According to the correspondent, Miss Lester discovered as many as 116 Japanese people selling narcotics in Changli County, Hebei Province, and there were also 47 Koreans. Among them, 65 people had only resided in the area since the beginning of this year. The narcotics they sold were very cheap. Once they were caught, they all used extraterritoriality as a shield and were able to go unpunished. In Leting alone, a place with a population of only 30,000, there were as many as 200 narcotics shops set up by Japanese and Koreans. Workers in the mining areas of Tangshan and Guye were particularly severely affected by narcotics. According to reliable sources, there were as many as 550 narcotics shops opened in Tangshan City in the past twelve months. The Manchester Guardian then published a commentary based on these figures, saying, "The increasing addiction of Chinese people is appalling. Japan bears a major responsibility. There is a lot of powerful evidence to prove that the narcotics that Chinese people are addicted to are mostly transported from or through Japanese territories, and they are promoted in North China with the consent of Japanese officials. Any fair-minded observer who sees this situation cannot help but raise the following question: Since the Japanese army harbors ambitions for the provinces south of the Great Wall, is the open sale of these narcotics, which can make the will of the Chinese people decline and be unable to resist Japanese expansionism, being encouraged by the Japanese army?" (17th, Havas Telegram)

Foreign Secretary Hoare replied to an inquiry in the House of Commons today about the "Manchukuo" oil monopoly, saying that after Britain protested against the monopoly, it did not receive a reply from Japan. At the same time, the monopoly has been implemented. In this environment, British and American oil merchants have no choice but to withdraw from the "Manchukuo" market. He heard that the withdrawal conditions will be discussed by the British and American oil companies with the "Manchukuo" authorities. The British government's views on this monopoly and the Japanese government's responsibility have been fully documented in the note of April 29. (17th, Reuters Telegram)

Ambassador Arita: There is a Rumor that He Will Resign This Autumn: Shigemitsu Kui is Most Likely to Succeed Him.

In order to prepare for the naval disarmament conference at the end of this year and to refresh the atmosphere within the ministry, Foreign Minister Hirota has decided to resolutely transfer the heads of the ministry this autumn. Vice Minister Shigemitsu often has disagreements with the military and has formed a large force within the ministry, so he will inevitably be transferred to a foreign country. Therefore, the rumor that he will go to China to take up the post of ambassador is the most credible. Hori, the director of the Eurasian Bureau, will succeed as vice minister. The director of the New Zealand Consulate General will be appointed to succeed Hori. (17th, China United Telegram)

Anglo-German Naval Negotiations: Italian Reply Sent to Britain.

Today's newspapers reported in detail on the Anglo-German naval talks. The diplomatic correspondent of the Observer declared that when Ribbentrop spoke with Foreign Secretary Hoare last Friday, a basic agreement had been found, and the only unresolved issues were technical details in the agreement. The value of these talks lies mainly in determining how to conclude a broader agreement. No one in London believes that accepting Germany's proposal is a violation of the Treaty of Versailles, but it is not of great importance. The agreement passed by the Stresa Conference and confirmed in Geneva clearly assumes that Article V of the Treaty of Versailles has become invalid. For this reason, the British believe that the principles decided by the Stresa Conference do not conflict with the current Anglo-German naval understanding. The Times said that Britain's maritime hegemony is not as strong as it was during the war, but the political situation is quite favorable. What Germany is discussing now is the combat power of the two countries' fleets, which has become a usage rate. The two countries decide the combat power of their fleets based on each other's plans. It is very clear that Germany has no intention of fighting at sea in Europe. (16th, National Telegram)

According to predictions in newspapers here, the Anglo-German naval talks will soon lead to an agreement. The News Agency said that the Anglo-German talks are now proceeding on the basis of Germany's request for 35 percent. The Evening News claimed that, given the current situation, Britain has no objection to this, so it is highly possible that an agreement will be reached on this basis. The newspaper continued that Hitler has clearly acknowledged that the British navy should be superior to any other country except the United States. If other European countries want to expand their navies, Britain will inevitably expand accordingly, and Germany can also expand accordingly according to the British proportion. The only question now is whether this agreement can be concluded. The Daily Telegraph said that when the Anglo-German talks began, France felt deeply uneasy. At that time, MacDonald had not yet resigned, but since Hoare took over as Foreign Secretary, he has indicated that France has no need to worry and that the British government will not allow anything to happen that would frighten France. (16th, National Telegram)

Britain recently sent notes to the governments of the United States, Japan, France, and Italy, requesting that the naval provisions of the Treaty of Versailles be amended to recognize that Germany's naval tonnage accounts for 35 percent of Britain's. Except for France, the United States, Japan, and Italy have replied separately. The United States and Japan have given affirmative replies. However, the reply from Italian Prime Minister Mussolini requested that it be studied before a detailed reply is given, but he believed that the German naval issue should be included in the general German armaments issue, discussed together, and should not be treated as a special issue and resolved separately. Although the French reply has not yet been received, judging from the French newspapers' tone, the French opinion is generally the same as that of Italy. British political figures were quite shocked to hear of Italy's proposal, believing that if the general German armaments issue is to be resolved and the amendment of the military provisions of the Treaty of Versailles is to be legalized, it will inevitably take a long time. Even if France and Italy give detailed replies, an agreement may not be reached immediately. However, Britain and Germany can disregard the attitudes of France and Italy and conclude an agreement first to determine the naval shipbuilding procedures of the two countries. Afterwards, they should discuss the matter at length with France and Italy through diplomatic channels to seek a final solution. The British side hopes to hold verbal consultations with France to point out to France that Germany's naval shipbuilding procedures are not inconvenient and should not be overly concerned. It hopes that France will accept it first, and Italy will inevitably follow France to accept it. Therefore, after the British government receives the French reply this week, it will probably indicate that after the German naval representatives return to the country, it hopes that France will send a delegation of naval experts to Britain to hold verbal negotiations with Britain. (17th, Havas Telegram)

The British government consulted the Italian government last week on Germany's request that its naval tonnage should account for 35 percent of Britain's. It is generally believed that Italy has replied to this note, saying that Italy considers this issue to be extremely important and extremely complex. Therefore, the Italian government has to conduct a thorough study. The Italian government will immediately conduct a detailed study and then notify the British government of the results of the study. However, the Italian government believes that the determination of Germany's naval tonnage should be discussed within the scope of Germany's general armaments and should not be regarded as a special issue and resolved separately. As for Italy's naval needs and shipbuilding plans, they have been publicly stated more than once and there is no change at present. 17th, Havas Telegram)

Retaining the Shell: US Recovery Administration Reorganized: President Appoints O'Neal as Acting Director, Three New Agencies Established, Layoffs Underway.

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued an executive order today appointing O'Neal, Vice Chairman of the New York Guarantee Trust Company, as the acting director of the Recovery Administration, because former Director Lee Chibao resigned today to resume his law practice. President Roosevelt reorganized the Recovery Administration as needed and has now established (1) a Business Cooperation Department to assist various industries in maintaining automatic operating standards, (2) an Advisory Committee as an advisory body to the Recovery Administration, and (3) a Research Department to investigate the impact of industry regulations. The person in charge of the Business Cooperation Department is Conley, and the head of the Research Department is Marshall. President Roosevelt has instructed O'Neal, Conley, and Marshall to expedite the reduction of the original 5,000 employees of the Recovery Administration. President Roosevelt said in his order today that the amendment of the Recovery Act will be carried out as soon as possible to adjust the work of employees to suit the current limited scope. Future legislation is not hopeless, so the usual structure of the Recovery Administration should be maintained. Observers said that President Roosevelt's remarks implied that he intended to extend the term of the Recovery Administration and make the principles of the Recovery Act permanent when it expires on April 1 next year. (16th, Reuters Telegram)

(Washington) President Roosevelt today issued an order extending the outline of the original Recovery Act to April 1, 1936. At the same time, he reappointed O'Neal, Vice Chairman of the Guarantee Trust Company, as Director of the Recovery Administration, and Marshall as a member of the committee. The President also established a new Business Organization Department with Conley as its director. The department's responsibility is to assist businesses in planning self-regulation. Labor representative Bailey has been appointed Deputy Director of the Administration and a member of the Advisory Committee. Other members of the committee include Charles Edison, son of inventor Edison, Vice President of the Miners' Union Morley, and AFL-CIO member Green. When announcing the above changes, the President said that the layoff of employees in the Recovery Administration will be carried out gradually and indicated that he may soon ask Congress to pass some new laws to include those parts of the Recovery Act that are not yet comprehensive. At the same time, Congress is also trying to make this temporary measure of the Recovery Act more permanent. However, the government has no definite plan. It is generally believed that as long as there is still room for improvement in the Recovery Act, the overall structure of the Administration should ultimately be maintained. (16th, National Telegram)

US Secretary of State Speech on International Situation: New War Almost Inevitable, Arms Race is the Enemy of Peace.

Ann Arbor, USA Secretary of State Hull gave a speech to students at the University of Michigan today, mentioning the continuously deteriorating international situation, saying that he did not believe that a new world war was inevitable, nor did he believe that a major world war would involve the United States. However, he felt that the United States could not ultimately avoid the adverse effects of a world war. Some foreign countries want to change culture by force with their new political systems, but the United States has never destroyed the basic principles of democracy. He also said that any country that does not participate in arms limitation is hindering the progress of the world and should be abandoned by everyone. (17th, Reuters Telegram)

Mexican President Receives Public Support: Embarks on Organizing Labor Government, New Cabinet List to be Released Soon, Troops Gather in Capital, Former President Flees.

Mexico City Mexican President General Cárdenas today mobilized troops loyal to him to the capital, preparing to organize a labor government by extremely swift means. The list of new government personnel will be released tomorrow. Cárdenas's action is obviously the result of defeating former Mexican President and dictator General Calles. Since his term as president expired, Calles has retired to Cuernavaca near the capital. According to the latest news, he was threatened by the current president's military force and has quietly fled to another place. Currently, workers, students, and Catholics who support General Cárdenas are gathering in the streets, shouting slogans supporting Cárdenas and overthrowing Calles. It is heard that Calles issued a statement before leaving, saying that although he has criticisms of the current political situation, he has no intention of interfering. His tone seems to indicate that he will permanently leave political life. It is rumored that Calles will live in northern Mexico near California, USA in the coming days. (16th, National Telegram)

Mexico City Mexico is now a one-party state, and its only political party is the National Revolutionary Party. Last November, General Cárdenas, a member of the party, took office as President and organized the National Revolutionary Party cabinet. Its domestic policy is quite left-leaning, deeply protecting the interests of labor unions, and imposing various restrictions on the power of the Catholic Church. Therefore, it was dissatisfied with former President Calles, an important figure in Mexican politics. Calles has had disagreements with the current president for a long time. Recently, Gil, chairman of the National Executive Committee of the National Revolutionary Party, vowed to obey Calles's opinions. Therefore, the cabinet organized by President Cárdenas submitted its resignation on the 15th of this month. The cabinet is currently being organized, but the left and right factions are taking the opportunity to demonstrate and attack each other. The major labor unions of the left wing have organized a National Proletarian Defense Committee, preparing to form a labor united front to deal with various threats to restrict labor rights. The Catholic Church of the right wing convened a general meeting today, gave speeches, protested against the government's destruction of religious undertakings, and marched and demonstrated in the major avenues of the capital, with about 10,000 participants, but the police did not interfere. (16th, Havas Telegram)

British Captain Tests New Lightweight Aircraft; Capable of Traveling 300 Miles per Hour

(London) British aircraft manufacturer Captain Percival has invented the "Percival" type lightweight aircraft, capable of flying 300 kilometers per hour. Originally intended for travel, it was later modified into a fighter-bomber. Captain Percival recently flew his aircraft from Kent to Oran, French Algeria, in North Africa, and planned to fly back to Kent for dinner on the same day. The round trip is estimated to be about 5,000 kilometers. It is said that this trip is to prove the "amazing power of the new lightweight aircraft." (Havas, 17th)

Central Bank Governors of Various Countries Discuss Currency Issues; Believe Currency Stabilization is Not Yet Timely; French Representative Describes Financial Panic Situation

Capital of Switzerland Central bank governors from various countries held a meeting at the Bank for International Settlements to discuss guaranteeing currency issues. They all agreed that the gold standard group of countries had won the victory in the struggle with speculators. Persons close to the central bank governors of various countries expressed doubt about the proposal of U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau to convene an international monetary conference, believing that Britain would not be willing to consider truly stabilizing the currency before the parliamentary re-election. As for the implementation of currency stabilization, it only requires an understanding between the three countries of Britain, France, and the United States, and if necessary, the addition of Japan will be sufficient. (Havas, 16th)

Capital of Switzerland During the meeting of the central bank governors of various countries, the Governor of the Bank of France, Mr. Tanary, described the recent currency panic in France, stating: "The traditional policy of the Bank of France is to maintain absolute freedom of gold circulation. Therefore, in normal times, even if the outflow of cash is very large, the Bank of France will never raise the discount rate. However, the situation is different if gold flows out specifically for speculative trading. The currency panic in France began at the end of March this year. At that time, the Bank of France did not take any defensive measures because the outflow of gold was not large at that time, and it was also the time when the Central Bank of the Netherlands raised the discount rate. France did not want to raise the discount rate at the same time to offset its effect. Subsequently, from April to the first week of May, the average daily outflow of gold did not exceed 60 million francs. However, in the second week of May, the daily outflow of gold reached 85 million francs. In the third week, the daily outflow of gold suddenly increased to 500 million francs, and in the fourth week, it was almost 1 billion francs. In total, from May 4 to June 7, the outflow of cash from France reached 9.9 billion francs, of which about half was shipped to the United States. As a result, a credit panic occurred in France. Speculators rushed to close positions and absorb cash, and the premium on cash rose to as high as 6.8% per annum. At this time, the Bank of France had to take action. The first step was to raise the discount rate from 2.5% to 6% from May 23 to 28. The second step was to strictly monitor exchange transactions to ensure the free flow of gold. In this regard, the U.S. Treasury Department provided a lot of assistance, because at that time, U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau often sold U.S. dollars in the market to avoid the dangerous consequences of stopping the purchase of gold. The third step was to strictly limit bank lending. The Bank of England also assisted the policies of the Bank of France. Despite various restrictions, the bills held by the Bank of France increased from 40 billion francs to 80 billion francs in one month. From May 10 to June 7, gold reserves decreased by 9 billion francs, discount bills increased by 5 billion francs, and various accounts receivable decreased by 4 billion francs, of which current accounts decreased by 3.5 billion francs, and the amount of banknotes in circulation decreased by 500 million francs. The large reduction in current accounts was obviously due to the tightening of the currency market. Technically speaking, most of it was the result of speculative closing of positions. In addition, government budget deficits, treasury difficulties, and general publicity advocating the devaluation of currency were also one of the reasons. As for the present, the government has obtained full power to make up for the budget deficit and restore public credit. The government has now decided on various preliminary measures, which will be officially announced soon. Both the government and the Bank of France have the firm will to maintain the normal operation of the gold standard. The French government is working hard to prepare to restore economic balance through the path of stabilizing currency prices to restore international trade. We sincerely hope that it will be successful soon," and so on. (Havas, 17th)

Motorization of Artillery in Various Countries Around the World

Warsaw News According to Polish newspapers, the artillery of the following countries has implemented motorization:

France has fourteen regiments of light artillery, six regiments of medium-caliber artillery, forty regiments of heavy artillery, and five regiments of anti-aircraft artillery, all of which use automobiles.

Almost all of the British light artillery has been motorized, and the medium and anti-aircraft artillery has also been motorized. Every artillery brigade of the local army has a battalion of motorized artillery. In total, 50% of the British artillery has been motorized.

Italy has four battalions of motorized light artillery, about 66 battalions of motorized medium artillery, and 48 battalions of motorized heavy artillery.

Romania has ten motorized battalions, anti-aircraft artillery, and some other motorized artillery.

The United States has motorized its medium and heavy artillery. Six regiments of anti-aircraft artillery and three regiments of mountain artillery have been motorized.

Japan has fully motorized its heavy artillery, and 25% of its medium artillery has been motorized. (External Press)

International Commercial Telegraph - June 17th Reuters Special Business Report -

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price Today is 141 shillings and 2 pence, up 5 pence.

London Silver Market Today is stable. The spot price is 32 pence 1625, and the futures price is 32 pence 875, both down 25. India and China sold, and China also repurchased.

Montri Silver Today's futures opened sharply lower. The September price is 73.00 72.90, 85 pounds lower than the closing price on Saturday and Sunday.

Exchange Rates

British-American The London foreign exchange market was firm this morning due to better sentiment in the Paris exchange market and renewed commercial demand for gold coins. The British-American exchange rate opened at 4 dollars 93 cents 5625, 6875 lower than the closing price of the American-British exchange rate on Saturday and Sunday. It continued to fall 4375 in the first hour to 4 dollars 93 cents 125, and then fell 33125 at noon to 4 dollars 92 cents 8125. Then it rebounded slightly, and at 2 pm, the price was 4 dollars 92 cents 5625, 1 cent lower than the opening price.

British-French It opened 15 pounds lower at 74 francs 78. It continued to fall 9 pounds after the first hour and then fell 6 pounds at noon to 74 francs 63. Prices continued to fall, and at 2 pm the price was 74 francs 54, 24 pounds lower than the opening price.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market It opened slightly lower. After the news of the flood came, the price rebounded, and the amount of the fall was recovered. At this time, the market sentiment was quite stable.

Chicago Wheat It opened slightly higher due to better overseas telegraphs, but the market sentiment tended to be short, and the price fell. Later, due to the report of excessive rainfall in the west, the price rebounded slightly, but it was slightly lower than the opening price.

Liverpool Wheat Today's price continued to be firm. At 1 pm, the July price was 5 shillings 3 pence 125, up half a point.

Liverpool Cotton Today it was quite firm. At 1 pm, the July price was 8.38, 15 pounds higher than the closing price on Saturday and Sunday.

Rubber

London Today's market conditions continue to be stable. At noon, the trading price for July and September was 6 pence 1875, the same as the closing price on Saturday and Sunday.

New York Today's market conditions are quiet. It opened about 2 pounds lower, but after some purchases, the price rose slightly.

Securities

New York Today's opening was quiet, and the trend was mixed. Metal stocks opened sharply lower. Public utility and oil stocks showed a firm atmosphere before noon. The movement of other securities was mixed and tended to decline. The average price of the Dow Jones 30 industrial stocks was 29.08, down 9 pounds. Li Zhonggong Telegraphed the Sichuan Salt Transport Envoy to Discuss the Reorganization of the Sichuan-Guizhou Salt Tax

Guiyang Li Zhonggong, the Director of the Department of Finance, telegraphed Liu, the Sichuan Salt Transport Envoy, to discuss the reorganization of the Sichuan-Guizhou salt tax revenue, the abolition of the lead salt system, and the restoration of the co-funding regulations. The telegram stated: (1) Sichuan and Guizhou should cooperate to restore the co-funding, but it should be done in accordance with the chapters and regulations, with officials supervising merchants selling and taxing on the spot. The salt has a fixed price, and the merchants have a fixed line. It is the fundamental way to completely eliminate the accumulated malpractices of the Sichuan-Guizhou salt gang's business. (2) Salt is the main source of revenue for Guizhou Province, except for special goods. However, the revenue from special goods is bound to decrease gradually to zero due to the strict phased ban on opium. Afterwards, all government expenses will rely on the salt fund. Now that the Sichuan salt tax has been transferred to the central government, it will definitely provide overall subsidies to the cooperating provinces in Guizhou. It is planned to temporarily use 1.5 million as the standard for the recognized amount on the four banks of Rengong Fuyong, with an additional 50 cents for each package of salt affairs expenses, which totals 180,000 taels per year, totaling 1.68 million yuan. If it can be handled, the central and local governments can take care of it at the same time. (3) After the salt tax is taken over by the central government, the salt sold in Sichuan and Guizhou will not be taxed twice. (4) In the future, the salt sold in Guizhou should abolish the provincial organization, so that there is a glimmer of hope. (5) If the above five points are accepted, a location and time will be agreed upon to come to negotiate in person. (Central News Agency, 16th)

Huai'an Hail

Huaiyin In the morning of the 16th, there was hail in Huai'an, the size of eggs, and the autumn crops were damaged. (Special telegram, 17th)

The Peace in Peiping is As Always

Peiping Correspondence The Sino-Japanese negotiations have shifted from the Hebei issue to the Zhangbei incident. However, due to the southbound journey of Acting Chairman He Yingqin, the talks have been temporarily suspended. Japanese planes often fly over Peiping to inspect the transfer of troops. There are no problems with the security of Peiping. Recently, it has been peaceful as always. Yin Rugeng went to Gubeikou on the 15th to inspect and will return to Peiping soon. The situation of each party is recorded separately as follows:

The Situation in Peiping

Since Acting Chairman He replied to the Japanese request, the people's hearts in Peiping have been at peace. The Xidan Shopping Mall, Dong'an Market, Zhongshan Park, Beihai Park, and Shichahai areas have returned to a lively state. Although Japanese planes often come to Peiping, there is no action, so the citizens are still calm. After the City Party Department was abolished, the mass organizations automatically disbanded invisibly, and there were no gatherings for meetings. There are very few slogans in the alleys and roads. The New Life badges on the arms of the police are not worn uniformly. However, the New Life slogans are still hung high on the archway near the former Presidential Palace. All schools are holding academic year exams, and students are taking the exams with peace of mind. There is no organization of the student council, and even the alumni associations of various schools have no meetings.

Yuan Liang's Talk

Peiping Mayor Yuan Liang told reporters that Acting Chairman He had left Peiping for Beijing on the morning of the 13th to report to the central government on the diplomatic issues in Hebei. The daily affairs of the Military Branch were handled by Bao Wenwei, the director of the office. The security of Peiping is my responsibility, so of course, I am responsible for maintaining it, and there is absolutely no problem. However, recently, I often hear rumors that incite people's hearts, most of which are unrealistic and whimsical. If the citizens do not observe, most of them will be shaken by them, which is really a meddling of fools. I hope that the press will dispel and make rational judgments on this at any time, so that citizens will not be used and seek trouble for themselves when rumors come. Moreover, the security of Peiping is jointly maintained by the military, police, and constitution. The daily precautions are very meticulous. Although Acting Chairman He has left Peiping, the security of Peiping will not be affected in any way. In the future, anyone who harms public peace and order will be severely punished in accordance with the law.

Yin Goes to Gubeikou

Yin Rugeng, the Commissioner of Jidong, left Peiping by car for Gubeikou at 6:00 am on the 15th to inspect the recent situation in the Jidong area, accompanied by Zhang Qinglin, the captain of the first special police team, and Inoue, a Japanese advisor. After arriving at noon, he met with the commander of the Gubeikou Brigade, Mr. Ishikawa, and the captain of Ishii's unit, and gave instructions to Huo Shi and others, the director of the Gubeikou Office. He returned to Miyun that evening and will go to Huairou Zunhua counties tomorrow (16th) to inspect. After a slight delay along the way, he will return to Peiping.

Chaiyama Arrives in Peiping

Former Japanese Embassy Military Attaché Chaiyama Kenshiro (the predecessor of Takahashi) arrived in Peiping from Tianjin on the sixth train of the Beining Road at 11:05 am on the 15th. According to Chaiyama, he came to Peiping this time without any mission. Because he had just returned from a tour of Europe, he disembarked in Tianjin and took the opportunity to come to Peiping to visit friends from all sides. He will stay for three or four days before going to Shanghai to take a ship back to China. Because he has not been in Peiping for a long time, he does not know much about the current problems between China and Japan and has no opinion to express.

Japanese Planes Fly

Japanese military plane No. 23 flew from Chengde to Peiping on the 14th. At 6:00 am on the 15th, it was flown back to Chengde by the pilot Tanaka Seijyo. At about 9:00, a Japanese plane flew north from Changxindian on the Pinghan Line, circling over Xiyuan and Nanyuan several times for about ten minutes, and then flew southwest. It is reported that it was inspecting the situation of the Central Army opening south along the Pinghan Line. (15th)

Brightness Bank Liquidation in Progress; Ministry of Finance Commissioner Arrives in Qingdao; Shanghai and Tianjin Branches' Debts Owed to Qingdao to Be Investigated and Reported to the Ministry for Approval

Qingdao Correspondence: After the Minghua Bank ceased operations, Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie repeatedly petitioned the Ministry of Finance to dispatch a commissioner to Qingdao to expedite the liquidation of the bank's debts. The Ministry of Finance granted his request and specially appointed Commissioner Qiu Zhenglun, who arrived in Qingdao by plane on the 13th from Shanghai to supervise the liquidation. Mayor Shen hosted a banquet for Mr. Qiu at the Yingbin (Guest Reception) Hotel on the evening of the 14th, inviting representatives from the city's Chamber of Commerce, Banking Association, Liquidation Committee, and creditors to accompany him. During the banquet, they discussed the implementation plan. Mayor Shen briefly reported on the city government's handling of the situation after Minghua's closure and finally expressed three hopes for Commissioner Qiu's resolute leadership: (1) Expedite the liquidation process. At the beginning of Minghua's closure, there were originally two methods for handling the issue, either through court-led liquidation according to law or under the direction of the responsible Ministry of Finance. At that time, the city government convened discussions with court lawyers and creditor representatives, all of whom believed that court proceedings would involve extremely cumbersome liquidation and registration procedures, likely prolonging the process. Many creditors are poor and unable to wait. They hoped for administrative processing for speed, so a special telegram was sent to the Ministry of Finance requesting its leadership. Local agencies and legal entities organized a liquidation committee to first ascertain the details of the bank's assets and liabilities, to serve as a reference when the Ministry of Finance's official liquidation committee is established. This time, the Commissioner is ordered to supervise the liquidation. All procedures should be expedited to complete the task within the time limit stipulated by the Ministry of Finance, to satisfy the eager expectations of all creditors. (2) Make every effort to recover the large sums of cash owed to the Qingdao branch by the Shanghai, Tianjin, and other branches, as well as the negotiable securities transported to Shanghai, to compensate the city's debts. According to the Liquidation Committee's report on Minghua's business situation in the city, it was originally profitable. However, due to the Shanghai, Tianjin, and other branches misappropriating 1.8 million yuan in large sums of cash and transporting negotiable securities worth approximately 200,000 yuan to Shanghai, the assets and liabilities became significantly imbalanced. This money originally belonged to the Qingdao branch. If it is not recovered and used to compensate Qingdao depositors, fairness will not be served. Recently, there have been rumors that the Beijing branch will repay debts at 70% of their value. If this news is confirmed, it would be equivalent to using Qingdao deposits to repay debts elsewhere, which is illogical and unfair. It is hoped that the Honorable Commissioner will thoroughly investigate the misappropriation of Qingdao branch funds by the Shanghai, Tianjin, and other branches, and make every effort to recover the negotiable securities transported to Shanghai, to meet the needs of repaying the city's debts. (3) It is hoped that the existing assets of the Qingdao branch will be quickly converted into cash to repay a portion of the debts first. The bank's depositors, numbering nearly 10,000, mostly consist of poor city residents, or the elderly and weak women, who rely on this for their livelihoods. Once their livelihoods are cut off, it could lead to major social problems. It is hoped that the Honorable Commissioner will be mindful of the people's hardships and quickly find ways to liquidate the bank's assets in Qingdao, so that a portion of the debt can be repaid as soon as possible to reassure the public," and so on. After Shen's report, Commissioner Qiu rose to give a speech, briefly stating that Minghua's closure was undertaken by the municipal government, instructing the Social Affairs Bureau to seal the books together with local groups, and organizing a Liquidation Committee to ascertain the bank's asset and liability situation, so that he would have a basis upon arrival, and he was most grateful. Before leaving Shanghai, he had consulted the Minister and Deputy Minister for policy guidelines. He was ordered to come to Qingdao as soon as possible to supervise the liquidation in accordance with the Ministry's recently established six-point liquidation method. Once the liquidation shows some progress, he will report to the Ministry for further instructions. The three points raised by Mayor Shen are extremely important. He respectfully presents his humble opinions below: (1) Mayor Shen hopes for swift progress, and he greatly sympathizes with this view. As soon as the Liquidation Committee is organized and established, it will begin work diligently. (2) The internal affairs of Minghua, as well as the debt situations of the Shanghai, Tianjin, and other branches, will be reported to the Ministry of Finance for approval after the Liquidation Committee has thoroughly and clearly investigated the entire situation of assets and debts. (3) How to dispose of Minghua's assets in Qingdao will be decided by the Liquidation Committee after it has approved a plan, and he will then request instructions from the Ministry of Finance and follow them accordingly," and so on. (15th)

Fujian Province Improves Tea Production – Preliminary Plan Set by Construction Bureau

Fuzhou Correspondence: The most famous tea-producing regions in Fujian Province are the Northwest and North routes, followed by the South route. The West route is located in the upstream counties of northern Fujian, the North route refers to the areas from Fuzhou's Northern Ridge to Funing Prefecture, and the South route is centered on Anxi. Black tea is best from the West route, followed by the North route. Green tea is more common in the North route and less common in the West route. Oolong tea, also known as Yan tea, is best produced in Wuyi, followed by Jian'ou and other places. White tea, also known as Baihao, is superior when produced in Funing Prefecture. In the South route, Tieguanyin is famous, with the best quality coming from Anxi. Before 1916, exports averaged about 10 million yuan per year. From 1916 to 1928, it was a period of decline, with exports only exceeding 6 million yuan. From 1929 to 1931, it reached 20 million yuan annually, which can be considered a prosperous period. In the last three years, the tea regions have been occupied by bandits, the people are not living in peace, production has declined daily, and it has presented a declining phenomenon. The average annual amount is only 90,000 dan, with a value of no more than several million yuan. Currently, in order to promote the tea industry in the North route (Funing Prefecture), the Construction Bureau has established a tea warehouse near the fourth pier in Taijiang, Fuzhou. The purposes are: (1) To inspect counterfeit and wet tea. Mountain households use wet tea to increase weight, suppressing prices. Tea firms, in order to rush to the market, mix un-dried tea and transport it to the province, resulting in moldy tea leaves. (2) To inspect the boxed tea packaged for transport to the province. If the box boards are too thin, they will break during transit. If transporting over long distances, it is particularly unusable and must be improved in the future. (3) To inspect and verify the packaging weight. The weight of packaged black tea is not consistent. Even under the same brand, there are differences in weight. Foreign firms, when weighing, choose the lightest as the standard, causing tea merchants to suffer losses. The weight of green tea packaged in bags is also inconsistent. Even under the same brand, there are often differences of several catties. When selling and weighing, handlers can profit from it. (4) To chemically test tea samples. Small quantities of various tea samples are sent to the Science Museum for chemical testing, comparing them with the standard tea set by the Ministry of Industry. (5) To compile tea industry statistics. The types, quantities, and prices of tea transported to the province from various counties under Funing Prefecture will be compiled. (6) To prevent tea theft. In the past, due to the lack of tea warehouse facilities, all tea shipments were transported by ships to Fuzhou, unloaded and stored in foreign go-downs, transferred to small boats, and theft from the boats was common. Tea was sold at low prices to tea shops. Boxed tea was sometimes opened with thin knives, and lead sheets were inserted, damaging the contents. (7) To avoid damage from wind and rain. The tarpaulins on foreign go-downs and small boats were not tightly sealed. When encountering wind and rain, the tea leaves would get wet. In the event of floods, the danger was even greater. Now, with on-site warehousing, this concern can be avoided. The warehouse rent charged is extremely low. This is the first step in the plan. The second step is to establish an agricultural experiment station in Fu'an, under Funing Prefecture, specializing in research on tea leaves and other products. It has been discussed with the Education Bureau to convert the county middle school in that county into a provincial vocational middle school, offering tea industry courses. The Bureau will also work with the Second District Commissioner's Office to establish an iron factory in the county, engaged in manufacturing various agricultural tools. The proposed location for the agricultural experiment station is Shekou, and the vocational middle school will also be moved there. Shekou is a tea-producing area for Fuding, Shouning, and other counties and can serve as a model for future merchants. Once instructions are received from the provincial government, it can be realized. (June 15th)

Guangzhou Prevents Communist Bandits: Labor Institution Captures Communist Propagandists; Headquarters Restores Intelligence Team and Postal Inspection

Guangzhou Correspondence: Due to the recent economic downturn in Guangzhou, the number of unemployed people is increasing daily, and the society is generally depressed. Communist bandits are taking advantage of the idleness of the unemployed and laborers, secretly sending party members to infiltrate urban areas, promoting communism to the unemployed and working classes, or distributing reactionary printed materials, engaging in large-scale activities. Recently, public security agencies have cracked down on many such cases. At the end of last month, at the Second Labor Collection Center near Haizhu Iron Bridge in Changdi, a person suddenly entered the center in the evening to seek lodging. After socializing with the coolie workers inside for a while, he used his manipulative tactics, tempting them with small benefits, then promoted communism, inciting the workers to join. The impoverished were tempted by his money, and one or two were deceived. Later, someone who understood the situation reported to the manager of the center, who arrested the communist bandit, seized evidence and more than 100 yuan in cash, and handed him over to the Public Security Bureau along with the witnesses for strict interrogation. The bandit initially denied it, but later confessed and revealed the locations of several communist organizations. The bandit confessed that his surname was Yao, his name was Sheng, he was 23 years old, and he was from Lizhou County. According to the report, police detectives searched for the remaining members of the gang and arrested many people that day. At the same time, military and political agencies recently received intelligence that communist bandits have recently organized propaganda teams composed of men and women, young and old, to promote communism, and there is also a so-called youth female espionage group, composed of young women, who are skilled at socializing, using their charm to seduce people, infiltrating the military and political circles, making friends with high-ranking military and political leaders, with the aim of gathering military secrets and political intelligence, and buying off disgruntled people for their own use. After receiving the report, the authorities issued orders to all subordinate agencies to take strict precautions, and ordered the Gendarmerie Headquarters and the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau to purchase more informants and intensify investigations. Previously, the Headquarters had a political intelligence team, which was abolished due to government downsizing. However, recently, in order to prevent the spread of communist bandits, the Headquarters has established an intelligence team of dozens of members, led by a captain, directly under the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters, specializing in investigating and arresting communist bandits and reactionary elements. Regarding transportation, postal inspection has recently been restored. Suspicious letters are intercepted and inspected before being allowed to be delivered. The Headquarters dispatched four lieutenant officers yesterday to be stationed permanently at the Guangdong Postal Administration to carry out the duty of inspecting mail. (June 12th)

Overview of Guangdong Railways: Business on Each Line is Not What it Used to Be; Zhushao Road Constructed to Luojiadu

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, with the collapse of the social economy, not only is business declining, but also transportation agencies are experiencing a sharp decline in revenue. Therefore, railway bureaus are introducing reforms to both management and business. An overview of each line is as follows:

Guangdong-Kowloon Railway: This railway, from Guangzhou to Hong Kong, is jointly operated by China and Britain, divided into Chinese and British sections. After the revision of the railway agreement last year, it was hoped that the railway business would develop. However, in reality, it has presented a bleak picture. The main reasons are: 1. In the past year, business in Hong Kong has plummeted, and the volume of passengers and goods has greatly decreased. 2. There are several day and night ferries between Guangzhou and Hong Kong, which are constantly traveling. Moreover, these Guangzhou-Hong Kong ferries have greatly reduced fares in the past month. Foreign shipping companies are selling passenger tickets for as low as one to three dimes. As a result, the lower classes traveling between Hong Kong and Guangdong are mostly choosing boats over land. The Guangdong-Kowloon Railway is affected by this and has no choice but to sell tickets at a lower price to compete. Its operating revenue has therefore sharply decreased. Currently, the railway's daily revenue is only over 3,000 yuan, which is over 1,000 yuan less than before. In order to remedy this, the railway is planning to expand freight transport, with the Traffic Department responsible for preparations. In order to meet social demands, it plans to charge low freight rates to attract more business.

Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway: This railway, formerly known as the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, is actually the southernmost section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. It was the first to be opened, with the route from Guangzhou to Shaoguan, passing through various counties along the North River. In the past, freight transport was the main source of revenue, such as cattle, timber, stone mines, firewood, rice, salt, etc. However, due to repeated natural disasters in the rural areas along the North River, people's livelihoods are extremely strained, and production along the route has greatly decreased. The remaining products are transported by waterways, which are cheaper. As a result, very few goods are transported by train. Secondly, the Guangdong salt industry relies on the North River as a hub, with its major sales markets in southern Hunan. Recently, Guangdong salt in southern Hunan has been taken over by Huai salt, resulting in a sharp decline in the volume of salt transported by train. The railway has therefore lost a major source of revenue. In summary, due to various reasons, the Guangzhou-Shaoguan Railway's business is declining daily. Therefore, there are talks of reorganization. It is heard that the reorganization method will start with downsizing to balance revenue and expenditure.

Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway: Originally a branch line of the southern section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, the route is from Guangzhou to Sanshui, passing through Nanhai, Foshan, and Sanshui. In its heyday, it was the most profitable railway in China, because the route was short and the fares were high. However, recently, it also has sighed at the difference between the past and the present. The fundamental impact is due to the decline of industry and the bankruptcy of rural areas in Nanhai and Foshan. In addition, the development of other

Page 8

water and land transportation means that the Guangzhou-Sanshui Railway is no longer a monopoly. Since the Jiangmen-Foshan Highway was built, long-distance buses can be taken from Foshan to Jiangmen. At the same time, the number of private ferries from Guangzhou to Foshan is increasing daily, with low fares, only one-third of the Guangzhou-Sanshui train fare. With the people impoverished and resources exhausted, and with tight household budgets, it is inevitable that travelers will choose water transportation. Therefore, the Guangzhou-Sanshui train is also planning to reduce fares to compete with the ferries. Recently, fourth-class cars have been added, charging the lowest fares. Normally, the minimum fare from Guangzhou to Sanshui is 30 cents, but now it is only 15 cents. However, there is still little improvement. The Bureau is currently trying to find ways to remedy this.

Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway: This railway, from Shaoguan in Guangdong to Zhuzhou in Hunan, is the Guangdong-Hunan border section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway and has not yet been fully opened. The Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Railway Bureau has been established to oversee the construction project. However, the Guangdong-Hunan border is a region of high mountains and ridges, requiring tunnels, making the project large-scale. Currently, the section from Shaoguan to Lechang has been opened. Recently, the track laying project from Lechang Qimen to Luojiapu Station has also been completed, and a trial run can be conducted on the 15th of this month. According to the investigation, the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section, from Shaoguan to Zhuzhou, is divided into 32 stations. Construction of each station is underway, and the names of each station have also been determined as follows: Shaoguan Station, Libutou Station, Yangxi Station, (the word "Station" is omitted below) Lechang, Qimen, Luojiadu, Jinjiling, Baishidu, Taipingli, Dengjiatang, Xiawan, Liuchuan, Xujiadong, Qifengdu, Gaotingsi, Liupingxu, Xiaoshuipo, Leiyang, Zheqiao, Wayuan, Guanyinqiao, Dongyangdu, Hengzhou, Dabao, Xiasi, Hengshan, Shangwan, Zhuting, Gantian, Zhaoling, Sanmen, Zhuzhou. (June 14th)

Qufu: Yansheng Duke's Mansion Must Be Protected; Executive Yuan Sends Letter to Shandong Provincial Government for Detailed Plans; Provincial Government Has Assigned to Civil Affairs and Education Bureaus for Review

Jinan Correspondence: Qufu is the birthplace of Confucius and the final resting place of his body. To this day, the mausoleum and temple stand majestically, the descendants of the lineage reside there, and the traces of the sage are numerous. They are closely related to our country's history and culture and should be cherished and protected. Therefore, by tradition, special protection is ordered. Since the central government issued an order granting Kong Decheng, the 76th generation descendant of the direct line, the title of Sacrificial Official, the name of the Yansheng Duke's Mansion has not yet been changed. As for the maintenance of security in the holy land and the preservation of cultural relics in the Temple of Confucius, these are the urgent tasks at present. In view of this, the central government, through the Ministry of Interior, has presented various measures on correcting the name of the Yansheng Duke's Mansion and establishing police organs, and has submitted them to the Executive Yuan for review. The Executive Yuan believes that the province has many old cases to investigate and should be handed over to the provincial government for planning. Therefore, it specially sent a letter to the provincial government requesting detailed plans and replies. After receiving the letter, the provincial government submitted it to the provincial government affairs meeting on the 14th for discussion, resolving to assign it to the Civil Affairs and Education Bureaus for review and reply. The Executive Yuan's official letter stated: "Having received the Premier's order, we have reviewed the Ministry of Interior's presentation on correcting the name of the Yansheng Duke's Mansion, establishing police organs, maintaining security in the holy land, and preserving the cultural relics of the Temple of Confucius, requesting instructions. It should be investigated whether the security within the official residence includes the forest and temple, and according to the organizational outline of the police bureaus at all levels, the police organs should be established. Whether the organs should be established within the official residence has been referred to the Ministry of Interior for investigation and reply. Now, according to the Ministry's reply to the above points, it should be handed over to the Shandong Provincial Government for detailed plans and replies," and so on. (14th)

Kong Xiangrong Convenes Henan River Engineering Conference; Eight Hazardous Projects to Be Repaired Immediately, Working Day and Night

Kaifeng Correspondence: Kong Xiangrong, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council's Water Conservancy Committee and Deputy Director of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, was ordered to inspect the emergency defense projects for the aftermath of the Yellow River in Henan, Shandong, and Hebei provinces. A few days ago, he rushed to the Wen, Yu, Zhongrong, Qin, and Chenqiao areas in Henan Province, examining the dangerous sections of the valley embankment one by one, inspecting them in detail, and deciding to immediately go to Hebei and Shandong provinces to continue the inspection and investigate the issue of guiding the Yellow River entrance. It has been reported in detail in various newspapers. It is now learned that after inspecting the various inspection projects in Henan Province, Mr. Kong deeply felt that with the imminent flood, it was necessary to actively concentrate, unite, and confer in order to expedite progress. On the morning of the 10th of this month, at 10 a.m., he invited relevant agencies to hold a meeting at the Relief Work Group in Bian. Those present included Fang Qidao, Secretary-General of the Henan Provincial Government, Wei Xigeng, Representative Secretary, Zhang Jingyu, Director of the Construction Bureau, Yin Renxian, Director of the Finance Bureau, Dong Zhaolin, Chairman of the Henan Yellow River Qinhuai Work Material Collection Committee, Chen Ruzhen, Director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, Zhang Hanying, Secretary-General of the Yellow River Conservancy Commission, Wang Yujun, Secretary of the Work Relief Group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, and Chief Engineer Fu Pucheng. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Kong. After a long period of discussion, the following measures were agreed upon: 1. Zhongmu Embankment and Bank Revetment Consolidation Project, 2. Chenqiao Embankment Doubling Project, 3. Chenlan and Lankao Flood Doubling and Repair Project, 4. Wuwen and Wuzhi Flood Bank Revetment Project, 5. Wuzhi Laoche River Embankment Sluice Gate Project, 6. Yellow River North and South Bank Embankment Consolidation Project, 7. Qinhuai River Bank Revetment Project, 8. Huaxian Lao'an Embankment Follow-up Project. For the above projects, except for the seventh item, which will be expedited by the Yellow River Conservancy Commission to transport stone materials, the first to sixth items and the eighth item will be intensified by the Henan River Affairs Bureau according to the results of the meeting. The Yellow River Qinhuai Material Collection Committee will expedite the purchase and transportation of materials, and the Finance Bureau will allocate funds in a timely manner. All eight projects will be repaired immediately, working day and night, in order to unite forces, promote progress, and consolidate river defenses. The meeting adjourned at 12 o'clock. Mr. Kong then went to Tai, Jiugulu, Fenglou, and turned to Hebei and Shandong provinces along the river for inspection that evening.

Suzhou: Zhenru Murder Case Appeals Hearing

The case of Zhou Pingyuan, director of the Shanghai Zhenru Police Station, and Xing Guonong, an employee, being accused of using torture to force confessions and causing a person's death, was judged by the Shanghai Court. Zhou Xie were each sentenced to ten years in prison. Zhou and Xing did not accept the original sentence and appealed to the High Court. The presiding judge of the Third Criminal Division opened the trial. Eastern Tai Lake Migrant People Run Rampant

There are a total of five or six thousand migrants in the Eastern Tai Lake who are enclosing lake fields. A portion of the migrants from the Kainand Company have been provided with funds by the company and dispersed. However, after receiving the funds, the migrants did not return to their native Shandong, but remained around Tai Lake and other places, running rampant, stealing items from farmers. Because of their large number, the villagers fear them like tigers. Changzhou: Chamber of Commerce Discusses Business Tax Issues

The Wuyi County Chamber of Commerce convened representatives from various industries on the afternoon of the 16th to discuss business tax issues. More than 90 people attended. Yu Yiqin was publicly elected chairman. Items for discussion included: (1) How should we respond to the notification from the Business Tax Bureau to submit the 24th year report within a limited time? It was resolved that the tax amounts in the notification are mostly inconsistent with the facts, and the following points of doubt should be raised to the Business Tax Bureau for auditing: (A) The various industries that are taxed according to capital amount have increased by more than ten times, which is clearly inconsistent with the facts. (B) Various industries’ credit collateral loans are temporary activities in this economically difficult period and cannot be used as fixed capital. (C) This audit mistakenly included various tax-exempt goods within the scope of taxation. (D) This audit mostly used the seasonal income and busy months as the standard for the whole year's taxation. The above points should be addressed by the Chamber in a letter to the Business Tax Bureau for correction. (2) With the business of various industries declining, is it necessary to elect representatives to state the difficulties to the Business Tax Bureau and request a reduction in the tax amount in order to alleviate the merchants' difficulties? It was resolved to publicly elect Wan Xiangyao, Cha Binchu, Tan Xianglin, Jiang Panfa, Lin Qiaobao, Yu Yiqin, Gao Yongni, Cao Rongzu, Zhou Jingsheng, and Shi Rubing to petition the Business Tax Bureau.

Wuxi: Compromise Method Decided for Wheat Inspection

In order to promote the purchase and use of domestic wheat and improve its quality, the Shanghai Flour and Miscellaneous Grains Trade Association specially jointly organized a Wheat Research Association to engage in research and improvement, and to inspect goods and prevent the addition of ash and impurities. Previously, the Association sent Ge Jixian, general manager, and Gu Leshan, an employee, to Wuxi to contact flour mills and rice merchants to promote the organization. Yesterday, Ge came to Wuxi from Shanghai together with Wang Yaochen, a Shanghai flour tycoon and a native of Wuxi, to negotiate with Rong Desheng, Cai Jiansan, Zhao Zixin, Zheng Yunxiang, Chen Hongyuan, etc. again. As a result, the expenses of the Wuxi Wheat Research Association will be advanced by the Shanghai Association as a trial. The original proposal of the flour mills paying an annual membership fee of 200 yuan and charging merchants one cent per dan will not be collected for the time being. Regarding the issue of wheat inspection, because experts are afraid of causing misunderstandings among merchants and causing disputes, a compromise method was adopted. It was decided that the goods stored in the factory's warehouse must undergo inspection procedures, while retail goods from passenger ships and rural goods are exempt from inspection. Rural goods that are more than 100 dan must be inspected by the Association. If the goods on the passenger ships are purchased by the flour mills, the mills will handle the inspection procedures themselves.

Various Yarn Factories Successively Reduce Working Hours

Due to the impact of cheap yarn and expensive cotton, coupled with the influence of the North China situation, tight credit, and difficult financial turnover, various yarn factories in this county have decided to implement a reduction in working hours. The Zhenxin Yarn Factory outside Ximen has already implemented a 25% reduction in working hours. The Yukang Yarn Factory in Lihuazhuang outside Beimen also reduced working hours by 50% starting yesterday (the 17th), and completely suspended night shifts. Male and female workers on day and night shifts take turns working three days each week, and continue to observe four days of holiday work each week as before. The reduction in working hours at this factory is greater than that at Zhenxin. The reason for this is not only due to the suffering felt by the entire yarn industry but also related to the weather. The river in front of the factory gate is unusually shallow and difficult to draw water from, so they have no choice but to do so. The Shenxin No. 3 Factory in Taibaodun, Xidou, is currently discussing the issue of reducing working hours with Rong Desheng, Xue Mingjian, and others, and plans to reduce the number of yarn spindles in operation by 10,000, but this will reduce the work of the workers without laying them off. Other factories, such as Guangqin, Fuxing, etc., have not yet implemented a reduction in working hours.

Farmer Unearths Golden Wine Cups While Weeding Field

Guo Fulin, a villager from Tangjiaqiao outside the east gate of this city, is engaged in farming and has a modest livelihood. Due to the poor silk harvest this year, he converted the mulberry field next to his house into a rice paddy a few days ago. Suddenly, he unearthed twelve golden wine cups in the soil, each weighing eight taels, and a golden soup ladle weighing seven taels, totaling one hundred and three taels. The wine cups were also stamped with a fire brand. Guo Fulin was overjoyed after unearthing them and is secretly keeping them to himself, claiming that they are copper wine cups and not gold.

Flying Silk Falls in Shitangwan

Yesterday (the 17th) at around 11:00 AM, in Shitangwan Town, in the tenth district of this county, flying silk suddenly fell in the sunlight. It was white and soft, either in circles or long shapes, in various forms. Because the texture was very light, it was difficult to pick up after landing, but it was easy to pick up on telephone poles, etc. It stopped at 2:30 PM. The surrounding three or four li of the town were all covered with it. The villagers were all amazed. However, according to old farmers, what fell may be "heavenly silk" or "earthly silk," so it is recorded for the study of geographers.

Since the beginning of summer, this county has experienced scarce rainfall. At this time of year when farmers are transplanting rice seedlings, water is greatly needed. Unexpectedly, for days on end, the sun blazed and there was no sign of rain, and the fields were cracked. The farmers were extremely worried. On the morning of the 16th, the weather changed and a sudden rain shower fell, stopping at noon. In the afternoon, there was more light rain. Agricultural work is expected to be worry-free.

Haimen: Prolonged Drought Threatens Disaster

Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been a prolonged drought. Crops such as cotton and beans in various villages are suffering from withering due to lack of rain, as they have only recently sprouted and are only one or two inches above the ground. In the five or six districts of Xiasha, due to the dry soil, most of the various crops have not been planted. The river water is also gradually becoming shallow, and residents are panicked about drinking water. If there is still no rain this month, a drought will be unavoidable. Farmers, mindful of the painful drought last year, are all showing signs of worry.

Liuhe: Welcome Rain Saves Withering Crops

Since the beginning of summer in this county, there has been a prolonged drought. The transplanted rice seedlings were about to wither. Fortunately, at around 8:00 AM yesterday (the 15th), dark clouds filled the sky and there was a heavy rain that lasted for two hours, with more than three inches of rain. The dying crops are all expected to be revived. The farmers are all overjoyed. However, rice prices are still soaring, mostly due to a small number of unscrupulous merchants hoarding and manipulating the market.

County Magistrate Cao, in view of the importance of the third phase of inspecting Baodu, led Section Chief Wang and clerk Zhang and a party of more than ten people to Fanchuan and Zhangzhuang early on the morning of the 14th to inspect Baodu.

Letter

To the Shanghai Shen Bao Newspaper Office,

Having read the Nanjing special dispatch in the fourth edition of your esteemed newspaper on the 14th of this month, with the headline "Case of Unauthorized Lake Land Construction in East Tai Lake," which stated that the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, based on successive reports from the Wu County Party Headquarters and the County Farmers' Association, etc., claimed that the unauthorized construction of lake land in East Tai Lake was hindering water conservancy. Villagers, etc., participated in the demolition of the enclosure on the 9th and 10th of this month upon the order of the County Government, but only demolished one-thirtieth of it. On the 10th, Ah Qiao, etc., were beaten by visiting residents, and the security team protected the visiting residents and threatened them. We are especially re-telegraphing to the Party and government authorities to severely punish and stop the ineffective local authorities, in order to maintain the agricultural land and the water of Tai Lake in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, and to further request the Jiangsu Construction Department to investigate, etc. We are extremely surprised. Upon investigation, the County Government of this county followed the resolution of the Provincial Government and sent personnel to lead the villagers to demolish the enclosure. In a few days, Li Fuwei and other places outside the mouth were completely demolished. The provincial security team patrols day and night, doing everything possible to maintain public order. Recently, work has been temporarily suspended due to busy agricultural affairs, with no other reason. This department has never submitted a report on this case to the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission. This news is likely a false rumor, or even a deliberate fabrication by villains. We are especially writing to correct the record, hoping that it will be published to clarify the facts and distinguish right from wrong.

Sun Danbi, Wu County Party Affairs Special Commissioner (seal)

June 16, 1935
