Boy Shun Gu Kidnapping Case; Kidnapper Captured in Pudong, Victim Also Rescued

Shun Gu, the eight-year-old son of Ms. Chu Li, a Taizhou woman who runs a baked flatbread shop at No. 5 Yalü Road, disappeared suddenly while playing in a nearby alley at about 9:00 a.m. on the 30th of last month. She had people search for him everywhere to no avail. Between the 4th and 8th of this month, she received three letters with the name "Big Pockmarked Face" claiming that her child was in his possession and that she must prepare 3,000 yuan in silver dollars for ransom, otherwise, he would take drastic measures. He also threatened the father, saying that if he played games, he would use a pistol. Ms. Chu knew that "Big Pockmarked Face" was her fellow villager Sun Baoquan (29 years old), who had worked in her shop last autumn but had been dismissed due to some reason. He had accumulated hatred. Initially, she dared not report it to the police, fearing that her husband would be poisoned. It was not until the 14th that she reported the situation to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. The case was investigated by Chinese detective Wang Chengying of the General Inspectorate, who learned that the suspect Sun was hiding at No. 8 Daqing Street, Fukang Road, Pudong. He rushed there the day before yesterday and, together with detectives from the local Public Security Bureau, arrested Sun at the address. Under interrogation, he learned that Chu's child was living with Yao Ajin, a friend of hers, in Yujia Temple, Yangjiadu. Only a piece of clothing and a pair of wooden slippers worn by the child were found in the house. Detective Wang escorted the suspect Sun to Yao's house to find the child. They met Yao on the way, who had heard the news and fled. He took him along with Chu's child across the river to Pudong and brought them to the Jiaxing Road Police Station. The captain ordered him to be detained. The child was taken back by his mother. Yesterday, the farm, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. Lawyer Wang Yaotang of the Public Concession elaborated on the previous situation and filed a public prosecution according to Article 1 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits for the crime of extortion. He also stated that the defendant said in the police station that the three letters were written at a fortune-telling stall on Huishan Road and would be presented for inspection. Next, Detective Wang reported the process of solving the case. Chu's child said that he was tricked by the defendant into buying candy somewhere and was taken to Pudong. He was beaten from time to time to prevent him from speaking out. There were many wounds on his buttocks and chest, which were presented in court for examination. When questioned, the defendant's confession was vague, saying that there was another person who kidnapped the child. Judge Ye Shengchao ordered that he be remanded and scheduled for another hearing.

Middle-Aged Woman Throws Herself into the River; Rescue Fails, Joins the Water Gods

Yesterday afternoon at 4:30, the Taikoo Company's Kuai Da [Fast Big] first-class small ferry carried passengers from the Huatong Wharf in Pudong to the company's wharf in Puxi. When the boat reached the center of the river, a middle-aged woman handed a paper package to another man and pretended to go to the stern of the boat to urinate. In that instant, the woman suddenly jumped into the river and committed suicide. At that time, the boat was sailing very fast, and it was too late to stop the engine and rescue her. The woman died in the river and sank, her whereabouts unknown. The man took the original boat to the Customs Water Police Station to report. He said that his name was Wang Liansheng and he was a waiter at the Zhongnan Hotel in Shanghai. The deceased was about 30 years old and was from Guangdong. He did not know her name, but people called her "Guangdong Lao Wu". He knew a guest in room 503 of the hotel, and today she went to the hotel alone to play. At two o'clock in the afternoon, she asked me to accompany her to the Taikoo Company's Pudong Huatong Wharf to find a friend on the Suzhou boat, but she couldn't find him. We took the Kuai Da small ferry back to Puxi together. On the way, she handed me a paper package containing four photos. One was a picture of the deceased herself, and three were pictures of her husband. She asked me to send it to her sister Shi Aibao's house at No. 35 Maoyi Lane, Shanhaiguan Road, Baike Road. She also asked her sister to prepare two letters and send them to Li Xinglong Cake Shop on Ermalu Road, Guangzhou, and Zhang Yuanlin's house at No. 21 Yijing Lane, Chaozhou, Shantou. After saying this, she excused herself to urinate and suddenly committed suicide. As for why she took this dead end, I don't know. The police station observed that the man in the photos was wearing a suit, and the woman was wearing a black skirt and glasses. The couple looked like intellectuals. The detective ordered her sister to be detained and interrogated.

French Police Arrest Robbers; Detained Pending Investigation

French Police Detective Inspector Jin Jiulin, Detective Zhang Ziying, Deputy Detective Qin Youyu, Plainclothes Detective Ma Yizhi, and others learned the day before yesterday that a large number of robbers were hiding in the Dongfang Apartment at No. 415 Beile Road. They immediately went to the address and arrested the robber Xu Gengsheng (28 years old, from Chongming) in room 57 of the apartment. They found two pistols and 20 bullets on his person. They also continued to arrest Yu Jinxing (22 years old, from Pudong), Lu Shouzhen (21 years old, from Pudong), Yu Xiaomao (23 years old, from Yongren), and Wang Bingren (25 years old, from Nanjing) in rooms 39 and 41. They also arrested Yao Hesheng (22 years old, from Shanghai) at the overhanging building at No. 5 Guangxi Road and Yu Huating (27 years old, from Yongren) at No. 158 Hongdeli, Fangjiazhai, Chengdu Road. They were all taken back to the police station and detained. Yesterday, they were escorted to the First Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo questioned them. Police lawyer Tao Zhaodi stated the case and requested a two-week extension to investigate the case before requesting a trial. Next, Detective Qin Youyu reported the process of arresting the defendants and presented the pistols and bullets to the court. Under interrogation, the defendants confessed to robbing several properties, including No. 180 Pushi Road. After verifying the confessions in court, it was decided to postpone the hearing to the 26th of this month, and the defendants were remanded.

Car Crash on Avenue Edward VII; One Car Crashes Through a Wall, Several Dancers Injured

At 2:45 a.m. yesterday, at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Chengdu Road in the Public Concession, a No. 12019 yellow taxi, traveling from west to east, collided with a No. 18186 taxi from the Sichuan Taxi Company, traveling from north to south. Both taxis were carrying six or seven dancers and guests. Because they failed to yield to each other, they collided violently. With a crash, the front of the car went straight into the wall of the Wanshenxin Sauce Garden at the corner of the intersection. The foot-thick solid wall suddenly became a large hole. Because it was late at night, the people in the store were awakened from their sleep in shock. When the police arrived, they saw that the people in the car were all frightened. Several dancers were bleeding from their heads, and those who were more seriously injured were immediately sent to the nearby Baolong Hospital for treatment. Those with minor injuries either went to the hospital themselves or went home on their own. Both cars were also damaged, but the drivers were unharmed. Later, Chinese and Western detectives arrived, placed the damaged cars on the side of the road, and called the taxi companies to tow the damaged cars back. The two drivers were taken to the New Chanzha Police Station for questioning. Yesterday morning, the police station dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to Wanshenxin Sauce Garden to investigate the losses. According to the investigation, the fire-resistant mountain wall at the entrance of the garden was completely damaged and had to be demolished and rebuilt, with an estimated loss of about 50 yuan.

Chinese Paper Mill Association Petitions the Ministries of Finance and Industry for Relief

The Shanghai Chinese Paper Mill Association believes that since the implementation of the new tariff regulations for imported foreign paper last July, the tax rates are lower than the old tariffs, resulting in a flood of foreign paper in the market, while domestic products are experiencing sluggish sales and significant losses. Therefore, they are petitioning the Ministries of Finance and Industry for relief, requesting an increase in import tariffs on foreign paper in order to maintain domestic industry.

A Summary of Domestic Bonds Published; The Only Reference Book for Domestic Bond Investors

The Xinxin News Agency reports that A Summary of Domestic Bonds, recently issued by the trust department of the Guohua Bank on Beijing Road, has been well received by the community since its publication. The book's material focuses on practical aspects, first describing the history of bonds, then the methods of investment and calculation, as well as the domestic bond market in the last three years. All winning numbers of government bonds, the number of government bond drawings, the highs and lows of market prices over the years, and the discount interest on bonds are listed in detailed tables, which are fully collected. The content is rich, and the binding is beautiful. It is truly an essential reference book for domestic bond investors. Each copy costs 50 cents. It is heard that there are not many copies of the book left, so please purchase them quickly to avoid missing out.

Letter to the Editor

To the Editor,

I read in today's newspaper about the telegram from Xi'an stating that several thousand bales of new cotton from the Shaanxi Cooperatives were shipped to Shanghai but could not be sold due to the impact of provincial currency. They are currently still stored in Shanghai. The stagnation of cotton sales, Shaanxi's only major product, has made it impossible to regulate Shaanxi's finances, especially affecting various cotton cooperatives. After investigation, the cotton shipped to Shanghai by the Shaanxi Cooperatives has been gradually sold, and there is not much left. The above news is not true. Please correct it.

Sincerely,

National Cotton Production and Sales Cooperative Transportation and Sales Headquarters

Sports News

Guangdong Province Holds National Games Preliminary Selections - Track and Field Athletes Begin Training, Swimming Selection Standards Established, Basic Team Members for Men's and Women's Basketball and Volleyball Selected

(Guangzhou Correspondence) The Guangdong Provincial Sports Committee has been actively preparing for the National Games to be held in Shanghai on Double Tenth Day in order to train Guangdong athletes to participate. Recognizing that the hasty selection of representatives last year, without sufficient training, resulted in a decline in performance compared to previous sessions, the committee deems it necessary to train athletes early in order to restore the honor of the Guangdong unit in this session. It also plans to submit a budget for participating in the National Games to the Department of Education for transfer to the Provincial Government for early allocation to cover expenses. The total cost of this participation fee is 52,621 yuan, which is divided into (A) training period expenses and (B) travel period expenses. Category A requires 5,400 yuan, and the remainder is for athletes' travel expenses, sports equipment purchase fees, clothing fees, meal fees, medical expenses, transportation fees, and athletes' pocket money for Category B. The training of athletes is temporarily undertaken by the Training Committee of the Provincial Sports Association. It has recently hired provincial and municipal sports experts as instructors for various sports, including track and field, ball games (soccer, volleyball, softball, basketball, tennis, and table tennis), swimming, martial arts. The athletes for each sport are mostly selected from the winners of the 13th Provincial Games held last month. Thirty-eight male track and field team members have been pre-selected, including six from Zhongshan University, seven from the Sports Academy, six from Lingnan University, one from the National Academy of Sciences, one from Xiangqin University, one from Aviation School, one from Yushan Middle School, one from Zhiyong Middle School, two from the Second Division, two from the Seventh Division, one from Huanwu School, one from Peizheng Middle School, one from Shunde Agricultural Vocational School, one from Shunde County, one from Heshan County, one from Far East Middle School, one from Zhongshan County, one from the Hong Kong YMCA, and one in an individual capacity. Twenty-six female track and field members have been pre-selected, including four from Guangzhou Women's Normal School, one from Zhongshan University, three from the Sports Academy, three from Zhixin School, three from Xiangqin University, one from Guangzhou Women's Middle School, one from the Guangzhou Municipal Sports Committee, two from Municipal No. 39 Elementary School, one from Municipal No. 41 Elementary School, one from Peidao Girls' School, one from Municipal No. 15 Elementary School, one from Zhenguang Girls' School, two from Zhongshan County, and one from Shantou City. The first phase of training for these male and female track and field teams will begin on the 12th of this month. Registration for swimming pre-selection members has already begun yesterday and will end on the 14th. The selection test will be held at the Dongshan Aquatic Sports Association on the 15th and 16th. The pre-selection performance standards have been announced as follows: (Men) 50-meter freestyle, 30.05 seconds; 100-meter freestyle, 1 minute 12 seconds; 400-meter freestyle, 6 minutes 10 seconds; 1500-meter freestyle, 25 minutes; 200-meter freestyle, 3 minutes 15 seconds; 100-meter backstroke, 1 minute 30 seconds. (Women) 50-meter freestyle, 42 seconds; 100-meter freestyle, 1 minute 40 seconds; 100-meter backstroke, 1 minute 52 seconds; 200-meter breaststroke, 4 minutes. The first preliminary selection will be held on the 15th and 16th. After one month of training, a second pre-selection will be held. The final selection will be held during the Provincial Aquatic Sports Games this year. It is estimated that the Guangdong Province will participate in the National Games with approximately 200 athletes.

(Further News) The Guangdong Provincial Sports Committee, in order to actively train talent and prepare for the 6th National Games on Double Tenth Day this year, has stipulated in Article 4 of the Provincial Games Regulations that "those who have achieved excellent results in the recent Provincial Games and have been selected must represent this province at the 6th National Games; otherwise, their amateur status will be revoked for one year." According to the Provincial Games Regulations, the province has already selected elite players from the teams participating in the Provincial Games to form basic men's and women's volleyball and basketball teams and begin training. Jiaotong University Swimming Pool Adds Elementary Instruction Class - New Tennis Wall Built for Practice

The Jiaotong University Swimming Pool in Xujiahui opened the day before yesterday. Many male and female students, faculty, and alumni have entered the pool in recent days. However, management is extremely strict. Those without a doctor's signature are not allowed to enter the pool to protect public health. For the sake of pool water cleanliness, except for female students, everyone is prohibited from wearing swimsuits. The pool water uses a sand filter circulation system, so it is exceptionally clean. An elementary class has now been created, with the school's coaches responsible for instruction at the designated times. The school has added a tennis wall for those who are new to tennis.

Baihong Liangxi Water Battle with Suzhou - Three Events Reduced, Two Large Silver Cups Split by the Two Teams

The Liangxi Track and Field Team of Wuxi and the Baihong Suzhou Team agreed to a friendly match, with the two sides exchanging letters for a long time. Only the 100-meter, 1500-meter, and shot put events were held in the rain, with mediocre results. The two large silver cups prepared as prizes for this competition were decided to be split between the two teams. Educational News

Ministry of Education Orders All Provinces and Cities to Formulate and Implement Compulsory Education Measures

In order to promote compulsory education, in addition to Minister Wang's circular to all provinces and cities, followed by the Ministry of Education's order to all provinces and cities to report on the distribution of compulsory education funds, more than ten provincial and municipal governments or education departments have responded to Minister Wang's circular (however, these are all specific situations without detailed measures). The Ministry of Education recently issued another order to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities, ordering the issuance of detailed rules for the implementation of the compulsory education outline. The education departments and bureaus are required to draft detailed implementation measures for all aspects of the compulsory education implementation rules based on the situation in their own provinces and cities, and report them within twenty days of receiving the document for record.

The Aggressive Implementation of Moral Education in Shandong Province: Fundraising Methods and Budgets Have Been Drafted; Provincial Government Cables the Central Government for Approval

(Jinan Correspondence) Regarding the province's instruction to implement compulsory education, with the establishment of twenty short-term primary schools in each county, totaling more than two thousand schools across the province, and an annual expenditure of 2,868,000 yuan, the preparation and planning have been detailed in previous letters. The Director of Education, He Siyuan, and the Director of Finance, Wang Xiangrong, have complied by drafting a budget and fundraising methods, which have been submitted to the provincial government. The content regarding the budget includes a recurring expenditure of 1,229,040 yuan, a start-up expenditure of 1,578,960 yuan, and a contingency fund of 60,000 yuan. Regarding fundraising, the Departments of Education and Finance have drafted three methods: (1) Military advances from the 18th and 19th years that are to be repaid to each county in the 24th year shall be entirely allocated to compulsory education expenses. (2) The 18th-year military advances that each county should allocate as compulsory education funds. (3) An additional surcharge on head tax (丁銀) will be added in the 24th year, with an additional 2 jiao 6 fen 6 li (角分釐) per tael (兩). The total amount from the above three items is estimated to be 1,854,579 yuan, which meets the Ministry of Education's requirement of raising more than half of the funds provincially. The remaining shortfall of 1,013,421 yuan is proposed to be subsidized by the central government. At the provincial government's political affairs meeting on the 14th, it was noted that although this fundraising was ordered by the Ministry of Education, the Executive Yuan had repeatedly issued orders prohibiting unauthorized increases in land taxes and surcharges, which is a matter of great importance. Therefore, the provincial government did not dare to make a decision on its own and resolved to cable the Executive Yuan in the name of the provincial government to request instructions for compliance. The proposal and budget from the heads of the financial and educational departments at the provincial government meeting are detailed below.

Proposal: Regarding the establishment of additional short-term primary schools for the implementation of compulsory education in the 24th year, the Executive Yuan, the Beiping Political Readjustment Council, and the Ministry of Education have all sent telegrams to the province, and this government has instructed the Shanxi (山) Financial and Educational Departments to draft appropriate methods. The Ministry of Education has also successively telegraphed the Department of Education to promulgate the "Outline of Provisional Measures for the Implementation of Compulsory Education" and the "Outline of Measures for the Distribution of Central Compulsory Education Funds for the 24th Year," instructing that each county should increase the number of short-term primary schools by at least fifteen to twenty schools, and that more than half of the expenses should be raised by the provinces themselves. Regarding the amount of self-raised funds, instructions were also given to telegraph a response before June 14th. Xiangrong and Siyuan, after consultation, estimated that with the addition of twenty short-term primary schools per county, the total expenditure for the 24th year would be approximately 2,868,000 yuan. The methods for self-raising funds in this province are as follows: (1) Military advances from the 18th and 19th years that are to be repaid to each county in the 24th year shall be entirely allocated to compulsory education expenses, to be remitted to the provincial government by the counties for unified collection and distribution, estimated to yield 432,372 yuan. (2) The 18th-year military advances that each county should allocate as compulsory education funds, those already allocated should also be remitted to the provincial government by the counties for unified collection and distribution, estimated to yield 621,207 yuan. Those not yet allocated shall be strictly ordered by this government to be fully remitted by all counties within a specified period (including the fourteen counties in western Shandong). (3) An additional surcharge on head tax will be added in the 24th year, at a rate of 2 jiao 6 fen 6 li per tael, based on 2 million taels of head tax in the province's 108 counties, estimated to yield 800,000 yuan. The total amount from the above three items is estimated to be 1,854,579 yuan, which meets the requirement of raising more than half of the total amount provincially. The remaining shortfall of 1,013,420 yuan is proposed to be subsidized by the central government to facilitate the implementation. Whether this is appropriate, a summary table of the expenditure estimates for the additional short-term primary schools for the implementation of compulsory education in the 24th year is enclosed for public decision. Proposers: Wang Xiangrong, He Siyuan.

Budget: Item 1: Expenses for adding short-term primary schools: 2,868,000 yuan. Item 1: Recurring expenses: 1,229,040 yuan. Sub-item 1: Teachers' salaries: 984,960 yuan (Each county is planned to have twenty schools, each school has two teachers, one receiving a monthly salary of 20 yuan, and the other receiving a monthly salary of 18 yuan, based on 108 counties across the province, the total annual amount is as above). Sub-item 2: Office expenses: 129,600 yuan (60 yuan per school per year, based on 108 counties across the province, the total annual amount is as above). Sub-item 3: Books: 102,680 yuan (Each school has two classes, based on a two-part system, each school can accommodate 160 students, each student requires 0.3 yuan for printing costs, based on 108 counties across the province, the total annual amount is as above). Sub-item 4: Inspection fees: 10,800 yuan (Six inspectors, each receiving a monthly salary of 100 yuan and travel expenses of 50 yuan, the total annual amount is as above). Item 2: Start-up expenses: 1,578,960 yuan. Sub-item 1: Construction expenses: 1,252,800 yuan (Each county is planned to have twenty schools, each school has eight rooms, seven rooms requiring 80 yuan each, and one room requiring 20 yuan, based on 108 counties across the province, the total amount is as above). Sub-item 2: Equipment expenses: 326,160 yuan (Each county is planned to have twenty schools, each school has forty sets of desks and chairs, each set costing 3 yuan; two large blackboards and four small blackboards, totaling 8 yuan; two lecture tables, totaling 5 yuan; one horseshoe watch, costing 1.5 yuan; one class bell, costing 0.8 yuan; one abacus, costing 2.2 yuan; one small dictionary, costing 0.7 yuan; a portrait of Sun Yat-sen, costing 0.3 yuan; three spittoons, costing 1 yuan; one school sign, costing 1 yuan; teachers' supplies such as beds, tables, lamps, and kettles, totaling 10.5 yuan, based on 108 counties across the province, the total amount is as above). Item 3: Contingency fund: 60,000 yuan (Proxy fees for female teachers during maternity leave, teacher incentive bonuses, teacher holiday workshops, and other temporary expenses). Note: If each county has public housing or ancestral halls and temples that can be used as school buildings, only renovation fees are required, and the above-listed construction expenses can be reduced.

Preliminary Measures for Promoting Moral Education in Anhui Province

(Anhui News) The Anhui Department of Education, in compliance with the Ministry's orders, drafted preliminary measures for promoting moral education in the 24th year, which were submitted to the provincial government for approval and then forwarded to the Ministry of Education. The measures are as follows: 1. Establish 1,220 short-term primary schools in the 24th year, averaging 20 schools per county. 2. Each short-term primary school shall have three classes, each class lasting two hours per day, with a one-year course of study. 3. Short-term primary schools shall enroll out-of-school children aged six to sixteen. 4. Each class in a short-term primary school must enroll at least forty students. 5. The curriculum of short-term primary schools shall be in accordance with the Ministry's promulgated curriculum standards for short-term primary schools. 6. Each short-term primary school shall have a principal who also serves as a teacher, appointed from those who have received appropriate normal school training or have served in primary school education positions. 7. Short-term primary schools should utilize ancestral halls, temples, or public housing as school buildings. 8. All out-of-school children aged six to sixteen in areas where short-term primary schools are established shall be required to attend school. 9. The number of short-term primary schools established in each county shall be proportional to the number of Lianbao (聯保, a form of collective security system). Each Lianbao (approximately 1,000 households) in the location of the school should raise approximately 75 yuan per year for recurring expenses such as repairs, lighting oil, tea, water, stationery, and miscellaneous expenses.

Zhu Jingnong Reports to the Minister of Education on Hunan Province's Compulsory Education Implementation Plan

Zhu Jingnong, Director of the Hunan Department of Education, reported to the authorities of the Ministry of Education at approximately 4:00 PM on June 15th regarding the province's implementation of compulsory education starting in the 24th year. The province's method for promoting compulsory education starts with the provincial capital and is generally divided into first-class, second-class, and third-class counties. First-class counties are expected to complete the task within four years, second-class counties will have a slightly longer timeframe, completing it no later than seven years, and third-class counties will have an even longer timeframe, ensuring full coverage of compulsory education no later than ten years. As for funding, it is reported that the province plans to raise funds from the provincial, county, and local levels, aiming to raise more than 500,000 yuan in the 24th year to fund the promotion of compulsory education, and will then gradually find ways to increase funding each year in order to gradually expand the program. Director Zhu will travel to Shanghai on the 16th, stay in Shanghai briefly, and then return directly to Hunan to plan the overall educational progress of Hunan Province for the coming year.

High School Graduation Examination: Important Matters for Schools to Note; City Education Bureau Issued a Notice Yesterday for General Knowledge

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau announced: The city's high school student graduation examination has been scheduled and implemented in accordance with regulations, and the relevant measures have been announced and implemented. However, this year's examination has a large number of participating schools and examinees. All examination venue order should be jointly observed. Before participating in the examination, each school should provide guidance on the examination rules to the participating students, and explain the meaning of the examination in detail to ensure that students uniformly comply and thoroughly understand. When participating in the examination on schedule, each school should be responsible for leading the participating students to the designated examination venue on time by the principal or the director of academic affairs. Report to the chief examiner, take care of each student to take a seat according to the compiled number, indicate the places for entering, leaving, and resting in the venue, manage the examinees to abide by the examination room rules, and must not hinder public order. For this year's examination, once the bureau assigns the examination schools, the graduating schools participating in the examination on-site will be jointly responsible for maintaining order. In the event of an accident, the school responsible personnel on-site will be held accountable, and will be severely punished according to the circumstances without leniency. It is hereby announced for general knowledge, and all public and private secondary schools participating in this year's examination in this city shall comply with the above, without fail. This announcement.

Physical Education Teacher Graduates: Track and Field Examination Held at Jiaotong University Yesterday; Gymnastics for Men and Dance for Women This Morning; Ball Games for Men and Women This Afternoon, Still Held at Jiaotong University

This year's graduates of the Municipal Physical Education Normal School held their practical skills examination at the track and field of Jiaotong University yesterday. Thirty-eight male students from Dongya and over one hundred female students from five schools, including Dongya, Southeast, China, Liangjiang, and Aiguo, participated. Yesterday's examination was on track and field, this morning's examination is on gymnastics for men and dance for women, and this afternoon's examination is on ball games for both men and women. The details are as follows:

Yesterday's situation: Yesterday's track and field examination included seven events for men: 100 meters, 1500 meters, high jump, long jump, javelin, discus, and 16-pound shot put; and six events for women: 50 meters, 400 meters, high jump, long jump, 8-pound shot put, and softball throw. For running events, four people were in a group and started simultaneously, reaching the finish line. There were eight timers, two for each record. For field events, women were divided into four groups, while men were not grouped. Each person had three attempts for jumping and throwing, and the best score was recorded. Overall, most students' scores were passing, with very few failing. Although the weather was hot yesterday and the sun was scorching, the students were still energetic and the judges were very enthusiastic. This examination was like a track and field competition between students from five schools and could well be called a sports meeting.

Today's program: This morning, men will be tested on gymnastics and women will be tested on dance. This afternoon, both men and women will be tested on ball games. Men's gymnastics will include (1) three different forward rolls, (2) headstand and triangular headstand, (3) back roll, (4) foot jump on the mat and other movements. Women's dance will include (1) basic body movements, (2) basic foot movements, (3) combined hand and foot movements. The ball games for men are soccer, basketball, and volleyball; the ball games for women are basketball, volleyball, and softball. Soccer tests four basic movements: stopping the ball, passing the ball, dribbling, and kicking. Basketball tests two basic movements: passing and shooting. Volleyball tests four basic movements: serving, setting, spiking, and passing. Softball tests five basic movements: throwing, catching, passing, hitting, and other basic movements.

National Salvation Ten-Person Group Supports Literacy Education Movement; Resolution Passed at Permanent Members' Meeting

The China National Salvation Ten-Person Group, established in 1919, has made significant contributions to various social undertakings, such as establishing free schools and founding national goods factories. Last night, in order to support the literacy education movement, the group held a meeting of permanent members at the cafeteria of the Youth Association on Sichuan Road, with over twenty people in attendance. Sun Daosheng was elected as the chairman, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Regarding the fund previously deposited in the bank, it was resolved to convert it into national treasury bonds in order to generate permanent interest, and Sun Daosheng, Zhang Jusheng, and Tang Hao were elected as members of the committee, with Zhang Jusheng as the convener. (2) Regarding the purchase of real estate, it was resolved to abandon the plan. (3) Regarding literacy education, it was resolved to elect Zhang Qu cheng, Tang Da sang, Zhang Ju sheng, Sun Sheng, Tang Hao, Weng Guo xun, Zhu Chang li, seven people as members of the committee, and Zhu Chang li and Weng Guo xun as conveners. (4) Zhu Changli was entrusted with the responsible to handle the date and venue of the next opening ceremony. The meeting then adjourned.

Higher Education Entrance Examination Started Yesterday; A Total of Ninety-Four Participants

The city's Higher Education Qualification Examination started yesterday at the assembly hall of Wutaishanshi Girls' Middle School, with a total of ninety-four participants. Yesterday morning, the first, second, and third categories all tested Chinese, and the fifth category tested advanced mathematics. In the afternoon, the first, second, and third categories all tested Chinese and foreign geography, and the fifth category tested advanced physics. Three essay questions were given for the Chinese test, and candidates could choose one. The questions are listed below: (1) Confucius once said he was happy to forget his worries, and also said that if people do not have long-term considerations, they will have immediate worries. Are these contradictory? Please discuss. (2) Mencius said to be happy with the world and worried with the world, while Fan Zhongyan said to be the first to worry about the world and the last to enjoy it. Are there similarities and differences between the two statements? Please elaborate. (3) Confucius rarely spoke of profit, while Mencius strictly distinguished between righteousness and profit. Is his statement still applicable today? Please elaborate. This morning, the first, second, and third categories will test Chinese and foreign history, and the fifth category will test advanced chemistry. This afternoon, the first and second categories will test political science, the third category will test educational history, and the fifth category will test foreign languages.

Graduation Examination at the Sino-French Engineering College

The Sino-French National Engineering College is holding its second graduation examination for university students from the 13th to the 29th of this month. An examination committee has been organized, with President Chu Minyi and Xue Fan serving as the chief and deputy examination commissioners. On the French side, Wei Zhiren, Director General of the French Municipal Council, and Louis An, Chief Engineer, were invited as examination commissioners. On the Chinese side, Zhang Yichou, Technical Director of the Ministry of Industry, Ao Jingji, Consultant of the National Economic Commission, Zheng Liming, Commissioner of the Construction Committee, and five professors and lecturers from the school were invited as examination commissioners. The important subjects for the examination are divided into civil engineering and mechanical engineering, including civil and ferrous architecture, surveying, mechanical construction, railway architecture, electrical construction, and electricity. This year's graduating students include eleven in civil engineering and four in mechanical engineering. The commissioners were very impressed with the students' examinations. The school was established more than ten years ago and is jointly run by the Chinese and French governments. It is an innovative institution among national universities and has a long-standing reputation for promoting communication between Chinese and French education and culture. It has sent students to France and Belgium for advanced studies on several occasions, and dozens of them have returned to China to serve in various fields after completing their studies. According to the school's regulations, the top student in each department will be sent to France and Belgium for further study at the school's expense. Moreover, the school's management is strict, and the curriculum and facilities are modeled after the French university system, so graduates become industrial specialists upon graduation.

Recent News from Pudong Middle School

Since Mr. Han Juemin took over as the principal of Pudong Middle School, he has been determined to reorganize the school. The admissions committee was established recently, appointing fifteen well-known teachers from the school, including Jiang Xianzhe, Wang Jimei, Wei Lizhou, Zhang Tiemin, Wang Jingzhi, and Lu Zulong, as members. The committee is currently proceeding with admissions matters and has sent people to recruit students in Beiping, Tianjin, Nanjing, Wuhan, and other places to select outstanding students. The school's original girls' dormitory is insufficient, and the new northern dormitory will be renovated and expanded in the next term. It is also learned that the first enrollment will take place on July 25th.

Fearing that misinformation would spread and cause misunderstandings, we hope that you will publish this letter on the newspaper to correct the errors. Sincerely, China Children's Culture Association, June 17th.

Tidbits

— (Yan Maode)

Truth is like an evergreen pine and cypress, a never-ending spring, and an indestructible cell in the human body. Therefore, truth is immortal and infinite. Grasping the truth can have the magic of turning white hair back to red, while deviating from the truth, even a living person becomes a walking corpse.

When we plan to do something, we should do it immediately. We must never miss the opportunity. If we wait until the time has passed, it will be too late to engage in it. Many people delay their lives in complacency. By the time they grow old, it is too late to work hard.

When the sun rises, I walk west; when the sun sets, I walk east. This is my life. Life tells me not to look back, but to look forward. However, I am always a person who cannot even see my own shadow!

Scalping

— Yao Fu

Each industry has its own "terminology"; especially the "lingo" of the petty ruffians and hooligans is particularly abundant. "Lingo" is synonymous with "terminology," but it carries some mystery and is similar to riddles and euphemisms. Terminology is a specialized noun. For example, the hooligans' terms for old widows, old crabs, nail tips, pretending to be fools, etc., are all different from the lawyers' terms for legal benefits, inheritance, quasi-incompetent, provisional attachment, etc. Aren't they all "terminology"?

"Scalping" is a specialized term shared by two industries. The scalping of petty ruffians is called "throwing top hats" or "catching turtles," and is generally an illegal act, like "pulling yellow cows" – pulling rickshaws across bridges – and "recording pig roe." Scalping by friends in the exchange involves skimming some profits. These are not the small-time thugs who "throw top hats," and have all the common sense.

The exchange is a legally sanctioned public casino. You shout loudly that "all industries are sluggish and it is not easy to make a living," which is simply foolish—whether it is short-selling or long-buying for three to five million, earning ten to twenty thousand is as easy as picking up a mustard seed. It is also easy for small clerks to do some scalping and earn ten or twenty yuan a day.

What is "scalping"? When friends on the exchange market hear some news—actually, it is equal to a rumor—and the price rises or falls accordingly, this is a wonderful opportunity for "scalping." Fleetingly, friends with nimble hands—called brokers or agents in the exchange—seize the opportunity, adding fuel to the fire and or selling fifty thousand, or buying a hundred thousand. Seeing that there is a cent or two of profit to be made, they settle at the current or next session. At least they can get fifty yuan or one to two hundred yuan, which is nothing rare.

Think about it, the exchange is open four sessions a day, and each session has fourteen or five categories, each with a minimum of two or three prices and a maximum of more than twenty prices. Isn't the daily income of the "reaching generals" in the exchange "bucks" "bucks"?—The exchange is of course especially "bucks" "bucks."

Because it is easy to make money, going to dances, dog racing, gambling wildly, and whoring excessively is not a big deal. And sharp-minded friends transform into wealthy men. However, taking concubines, building Western-style houses, and sitting in cars are always unavoidable, no matter how clever and stingy a friend you are. Because Mencius said long ago, "Food and sex are human nature."

"All industries are sluggish and it is not easy to make a living." What absurd and unfounded words.

Boating

— Chen Liang

Four people came out of the Wu Family Restaurant after having a meal, and then spent twenty cents at the bridgehead to buy a basket of loquats, a local product of Nanxiang, insisting on falsely claiming they were "White Sands" from Dongting Mountain. The peddler's shallow deception is truly infuriating. In fact, there's no need to blame the people of the interior; how are the so-called wealthy merchants in the city any different in their use of deceptive tricks?

We arrived at "North Sea," which is just a river. The boatmen call this river the "Nanxiang Port," which connects to "Shanghai" on one side and "Jiading" on the other. Boats carrying kiln goods, onions, vegetables, and livestock come and go all day and night, making the river surface very lively. There are dog barks, rooster crows, children's cries, and the laughter of men and women.

We envied the life on the water, so we hired two small boats. Zhu Shaofei and I rowed one boat together, while Wang Zhuo and Liu Chunhua rowed the other. An old woman steered our boat from the stern, making a "clink, clink" sound. The water separated and then came back together on our oars, separating and rejoining again and again. In this way, our small boat gradually rowed out of Nanxiang Town, and we saw dense tree shade, green bamboo, thatched huts, and fences made of thorns on the shore.

Wang Zhuo's boat was initially in front of us, but we soon overtook them, and they fell behind by about ten feet. Liu Chunhua took off his coat and rowed hard to catch up with us. Zhu Shaofei said, "We must keep moving forward, forward!" Thus, a competitive situation arose between the two boats unintentionally. This is just like society and life; the way of society and life is competitive, it is a duel, and therefore, the times are progressing.

Raindrops fell from the black clouds in the sky, and countless circles swirled on the river surface. Our progress was hindered, and we listened to the boatwoman's advice and temporarily rowed under a tree shade to avoid the wind and rain. The river surface suddenly became silent, with only the "beep beep" sound of rain in the bushes. We rowed our two boats close together, as if preparing to resist some kind of attack. We turned up the collars of our coats and leisurely began to smoke.

The Sky of the Future!

Little Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: A Special Enlightenment: Westerners Discuss Construction, But Regrets Remain; Ten Kinds of Longing

After he said this, he looked directly at Beihai. Beihai's face was turned that way, so Zhiqian couldn't see his expression. However, his footsteps initially seemed to want to move forward, but soon he retreated backward again. He stood still, not saying anything. The girl Yueying's dark eyes were darting around busily. Her body seemed to be stuck to the wooden door frame, leaning against it tightly. Thus, the two people didn't move for about ten minutes. Beihai seemed to be unable to bear it and stretched his knee, lunging forward. Yueying, who originally hadn't seemed like she would move, suddenly recoiled backward because of Beihai's reckless movement. Beihai took a few steps forward and saw that she had retreated and turned away, so he paused, stunned. However, after Yueying retreated inside the door, she didn't immediately leave but turned her eyes and smiled slightly at Beihai. Just then, voices were heard from the courtyard, Yueying answered, and then went inside. Beihai was very flustered by this and immediately walked out of the alley. Zhiqian stopped looking and quickly went from the back door of Little Western Heaven to the main gate, and then from the street at the gate, he turned onto the side street. After only turning the corner and passing two houses, he met Beihai head-on. Beihai was walking forward with his eyes straight ahead, as if he hadn't seen Zhiqian coming. Zhiqian had no choice but to stop and call him several times. Only then did he stop, his face red, and bow to Zhiqian, saying: "Mr. Cheng, are you out for a walk?" Zhiqian said: "Yes, I was bored in the hotel. Why haven't you come for tutoring these past two days?" Beihai smiled: "How can I keep letting Mr. Cheng fulfill his obligations?" Zhiqian said: "Your words are too polite and meaningless. If I don't fulfill my obligations, can't I still collect your nine dollars a month tuition?" (242)

Imperial Fragrance, Misty Record

— Originally by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

taking turns to play. This kind of delicate music was already very pleasant to listen to, but now on the water, with the gentle sound of the wind mixed with the jade-like sound of the water, it felt especially refreshing and pleasing to the ear. Although the notes were not particularly high, the more subtle and gentle they were, the more they stirred the heart and soul, making one feel very comfortable. And what were those two small boats for? They were like two kitchens on the water, carrying several small stoves and a group of eunuchs specially assigned to cooking, in order to prepare the Empress Dowager's lunch properly; this was what she had ordered in advance.

Li Lianying was still the same as before; no matter what the Empress Dowager did, whether it was a formal court ceremony or an ordinary banquet, he was always the chief commander in charge of everything. Naturally, he was indispensable on the lake tour. Zhang De, the chief eunuch in charge of tea and refreshments, also accompanied her on the imperial boat with two of his junior eunuchs. The Empress Dowager herself still sat in her throne with utmost dignity, with us standing respectfully on both sides.

"Ah! Coming to this morning, it can truly be said to be the ultimate in delightful and pleasing sights!" The Old Buddha said in a very gentle tone, praising as if talking to herself and as if speaking to us: "Therefore, one must not be solely busy with official business, but must set aside sufficient time for recreation."

Every minute, even every second, was very precious and joyful for her old self; she didn't dare to slack off at all, preparing to use all the time to enjoy herself to the fullest. Just looking at the expression revealed on her face, one could see it very clearly.

There was also a special decoration on the imperial boat that was not commonly seen outside: originally, on the central pole, it couldn't really be called a mast, because there was no need to hang any sails at all; it would be more appropriate to call it a flagpole. Apart from hanging a very large and beautiful dragon flag, there were also two long, narrow streamers, which were two sky-blue satin ribbons, blowing backward towards the stern of the boat with the wind. These two streamers were indeed too long; they could float all the way to the surface of the water, skimming over the wake left by the boat, swirling out countless circular patterns. Moreover, because they were already soaked in water, whenever the sunlight shone on them, they were truly as beautiful as a rainbow. (342)

Small Recipes

Tofu

— Nanggong Sheng

Tofu is an item that contains many nutrients. Eating it is both hygienic and beneficial to the body. It is an affordable and high-quality food, the most popular and beneficial food for the common people. As the weather gradually heats up, the dishes used daily should not be too greasy, causing the stomach to feel stuffy and bloated. There must be a refreshing and delicious food to suit the taste of summer, and tofu is the most suitable. Because tofu is a refreshing, tender and light food, as long as it is cooked properly, it can be made into many flavors of dishes and soups. Compared with delicacies from mountains and seas, it still feels more refreshing and incomparable to tofu.

Tofu comes in two types, old and soft. The old is harder than the soft. In the north, the tofu is all old tofu, a block like white stone, and you can use a scale hook to weigh the tofu on it. The hardness can be imagined. Suzhou has a kind of water tofu, which is kept in water and is even more tender than soft tofu. You have to use a spoon to take it out, similar to tofu pudding. Regardless of hard, old, soft, or watery tofu, all kinds of tofu can be made into delicious dishes and soups. The following are the tofu foods most suitable for summer.

Egg Tofu Pudding Use one egg to mix, mash forty cents worth of soft tofu, mix with the egg, first use one hundred dried shrimps, soak them in wine, cook the juice in a rice bowl, wait for the umami flavor of the dried shrimps to be exhausted before putting it into the soup, pour it out for later use, put a little lard in the pot and heat it until red, pour in the tofu mixed with the egg, slightly fry it, and it will become lumpy, then pour the dried shrimp juice into the pot, add salt, cooking wine, and MSG each a little, cover the pot and boil, until the tofu and eggs coagulate, and this delicious egg tofu pudding is made, the taste is fresh and plump, more than several times better than the chicken beans in Sichuan restaurants, and the price is extremely cheap, less than ten cents, it is truly a popular tofu food.

Fermented Bean Curd Dew Stewed Tofu Use half a bowl of fermented bean curd dew, add three pieces of soft tofu and mash them, add a little salt, cooking wine, and steam over water until the tofu coagulates. It is another extraordinarily fresh and refreshing vegetarian tofu. It is best to eat it in summer. It is a pity that fermented bean curd dew is not easy to get in Shanghai.

Pan-Fried Tofu Pan-fried tofu is a famous dish in Beijing-Sichuan restaurants. Cut old tofu into square pieces of about an inch in size and about two or three points thick, coat with egg white, put them in a lard pot and fry them on both sides until golden brown, add dried shrimp, MSG, soy sauce, cooking wine, white sugar, and a water scoop, cover the pot and cook over high heat until transparent, until the water is almost dry and the soup is thick, then the fresh juice of dried shrimp and MSG has penetrated into the tofu, and this delicious pan-fried tofu is made.

Raw Salt Tofu Add soy sauce, sesame oil or chili oil to a piece of raw tofu and mix it well. It becomes an incomparably refreshing raw salt tofu, which is a delicious dish to eat with wine or porridge. However, the soy sauce must be good, preferably shrimp soy sauce or mother oil. It is even better if dried shrimp and shredded ham are added and mixed together.

Stewing tofu with sauce, green onions, and white sugar results in an extremely rich and delicious flavor. However, the sauce must be homemade bean sauce for the best flavor, as it is fresh and pure. It is even more wonderful if chili oil and dried shrimp are added. It is a refreshing dish among summer foods. There are also many kinds of tofu foods, such as tofu soup, shrimp, crab roe tofu, and first-class tofu, all of which are extremely delicious dishes and soups. However, compared with the ones mentioned above, the prices are all expensive and not as popular as before.

Anecdotes of My Friend Mr. Wang

— Junmou

My friend, Mr. Wang, is from Beijing and possesses some assets. His father passed away early, and his mother is already in her fifties. He graduated from a polytechnic university and once worked as an engineer in Shanghai. He has a girlfriend, Miss Li, who is intelligent, versatile, and particularly healthy. Mr. Wang has always admired her. One day, Mr. Wang suddenly received a telegram from home urging him to return. When he arrived home, he learned that his mother, due to her age, was particularly eager for him to marry and have grandchildren. Because Mr. Wang was too cautious in choosing a spouse, he had not yet married. Now, his mother was implementing a forced marriage system, arranging for Miss Jiang from the same county to be his wife. She had used a pretext to telegraph him home in advance and had already chosen a day for the wedding. Mr. Wang could not bear to go against his mother's wishes again and had to bow his head and obey, completing the marriage. His wife, Miss Jiang, was indeed beautiful and healthy, and she had also graduated from medical university. Mr. Wang was happy to have such a good partner. Following his mother's orders, he stayed at home and needed to find a job in Shanghai. He took a position as an engineer at a factory in Beijing. After several years, he lost contact with his friends in the South, and Miss Li had also married. Later, the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, and Beijing declined daily. Mr. Wang resigned again and moved south to Shanghai, where he worked as a road engineer. He lived in a rented house with his elderly mother and beautiful wife. Jiang was also hired by a hospital to work as a gynecologist. While Mr. Wang was sorting through his closet, he accidentally found a portrait that Miss Li had given him in the past. He couldn't help but recall their past relationship and wanted to find out about her current situation. He showed it to his wife, saying, "This is Miss Li, a girlfriend I admired. I haven't heard from her for a long time." A few days later, while Jiang was seeing patients, she met a sick woman who looked haggard and seemed familiar. She found it very strange. Looking at the registration form, it was written "Shi, nee Li." Examining her condition, she had purulent leucorrhea. Because it had been delayed for a long time, it had affected her whole body, and her face was sallow and emaciated. Jiang immediately instructed her to have daily injections of the prescription to treat her whole-body diseases and also told her to go to the Tongren Pharmacy at No. 1 Dexing Lane, Xinjiao Street, French Concession, Shanghai, to buy a box each of external leucorrhea medicine and internal leucorrhea pills, two yuan per box, and to take them as instructed. While Mr. Wang and his wife were chatting, they mentioned this matter. When Wang heard "nee Li," his heart stirred, and he seemed to sense something. Jiang saw this and suddenly realized, "The sick woman in the photo you showed me looks just like her. I should ask her about it for you." The next day, Shi, nee Li, came for a follow-up visit, and her condition had improved. After Jiang finished treating her, she asked, "Do you know someone named Wang from Beijing?" The sick woman was surprised and said, "I do know him, but I haven't heard from him for a long time." Jiang said, "Wang is family." She then arranged a date to invite Mr. and Mrs. Shi and several friends for a meal at Mr. Wang's house. From then on, Shi and Wang became friends, and Jiang and Li loved each other like sisters. Shi had a deep-seated venereal disease, which Jiang introduced her to the Sun Weicai Father and Son Hospital at No. 64 Ningbo Road, French Concession, for appropriate treatment. Before long, both recovered their health.

Commercial News

Financial: August Futures Market: Gold Market Supply and Demand Remains Idle; Indian Silver Continues to Contract, Stimulating Buying; Initial Stability Followed by Firmness, Resulting in a Rally

Yesterday's August gold market was characterized by a lack of enthusiasm and scattered sentiment. With the transaction tax issue unresolved, major players continued to adopt a wait-and-see approach. The morning session was extremely flat, while the afternoon session saw a turnaround driven by the continued decline in Indian silver prices, which disappointed short sellers and stimulated buying interest. The morning began with a slight increase in overseas silver markets in London and stable prices in the United States. Deferred silver prices in Monte Carlo fell slightly by five cents to one and a half cents. Exchange rates saw a minor contraction. Spot gold in London rose by one penny. Reports of the Italian government nationalizing silver and prohibiting private possession of silver coins stabilized sentiment. Although pre-market trading opened with bids of 67.70 to 67.80 yuan, buying was more active, leading to a steady trend. Considering swap rates, the market was relatively stable compared to the previous Saturday. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with no change in both British and American rates. The customs gold unit rose by one cent, and the standard price for gold tenders increased to 835 yuan, with little impact. Immediately after opening, the market consolidated. The Bank of China offered shillings, causing a slight decline, but major players took advantage of the low prices to maintain their positions. It was anticipated that the HSBC's official rates for both British and American currencies would remain unchanged. Soon, the tide gradually rose, and exchange rates also tightened slightly. Buyers became more active and pushed prices above the 70 yuan level. However, banks took advantage of the higher prices to offer gold, temporarily halting the rise. Thereafter, sentiment became mediocre, and both buyers and sellers remained silent, resulting in a sluggish market with limited fluctuations, indicating an extremely idle situation that was difficult to stir up any significant activity. The afternoon session continued to be characterized by inactivity. The market only opened at 2:30 PM. Upon opening, the report of a 15 anna contraction in Indian silver prices stimulated buying interest, pushing prices above the 70 yuan level and rapidly rising. Banks took advantage of the higher prices to offer gold, leading to a period of consolidation after the initial surge. Later, the report of a second decline in Indian silver prices by another 2.3 annas further boosted sentiment, and the market closed higher again. Swap spreads narrowed, decreasing to as low as five cents, eventually settling around 1.5 yuan. A lack of short positions left buyers seemingly alarmed. The market conditions for the day are summarized as follows:

The morning opened at 768.5 yuan, down 2.1 yuan from the previous Saturday. Taking swap rates into account, the overall trend was flat. Fuxingyong, Qingfa, Yongna offered, rose to 8.8 yuan. Dda, Hui Xiang, Hengyu, Dadecheng sold. The Bank of China offered the first half of the August shilling at 6.25, retreating to 7.7 yuan. Later, Fuxingyong, Hongkang, Yongshunmao, and Hengyu stepped in, and the price rose to 0.05. Macali offered August US dollars at 0.25, Dadecheng and Huixiang sold, retreating to 69.3 yuan. At this point, there was still a rebound. Later, the Bank of England offered July shillings at 0.75, Jiatai, Rongting, Qianchangxiang slightly sold, Fuduo sold, and the price dropped from 70.3 yuan to 68.7 yuan. Yuanmao, Yongfuyu, and Fuxingyong stepped in, rising to 9.6 yuan. Macali offered June US dollars at 0.9375, Shunli sold, retreating to 9.1 yuan. Securities: Bond Market, Easy to Fall and Difficult to Rise; Turmoil Arises Again in the "23rd Customs Bonds"; Bulls Slightly Cash Out on "96 Bonds"

Yesterday, at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, because the situation in Hebei remained deadlocked and people's hearts were still uneasy, coupled with the fact that the general public was deeply deceived by reckless remarks, they generally held the principle of selling at high prices. Therefore, as soon as the market price rose slightly, it was suppressed by pressure. Therefore, it is difficult to be optimistic about the market situation. Yesterday, the market initially showed some progress, but eventually failed due to the above-mentioned reasons. Yarn and Cotton: Foreign Yarn Continues to Dump, Local Yarn is Severely Affected; Downturn Resumes After the "Thousands"; Prices Fall by More Than One Yuan in Each Month

The yarn market was flat in the morning and fell in the afternoon. The situation is extremely pessimistic because foreign yarn is frequently falling in price and being dumped on the market. As a result, people's hearts are shaken and Chinese yarn is severely affected. As for this month, due to the impact of economic recession, those who receive the goods feel it is especially difficult. Therefore, the market sentiment is quite weak.

Kim Chee Foreign Firm Massively Sells Off

The market for tagged yarn opened in the morning. Because it was reported that the incident in Chahar had been peacefully resolved, some shorts covered their positions and bulls actively bought. The market was able to maintain itself. As a result, prices for each month rose 10 cents compared to the previous day's closing price, and long-term contracts remained unchanged. When the market opened in the afternoon, it suddenly fell, and the decline became more intense. This was because foreign firms were selling off in large quantities. Another theory is that foreign yarn is being sold at a discount in the market, and the price of cloth is even lower than the price of yarn. Therefore, foreign firms are extremely pessimistic about tagged yarn, and the pressure is particularly strong. As a result, prices for each month fell by one yuan to one yuan and thirty cents compared to the morning closing price. Grain: Rain Brings Down Rice Prices Slightly

Yesterday, 27 shipments of rice from Southern Shanghai (a total of more than 5,000 piculs) arrived. Although the weather may be sunny and dry, it is unlikely to change color within these one or two days. Prices for all thick japonica rice have fallen by 30 to 40 cents. Although more than 300 packages of late rice from Qinhuangdao were sold, the price drop was not small. The price of Bian Yin Yuan was cut by 20 cents, similar to the price of Du Chien. (Northern Shanghai) Yesterday, although there were few ships from various routes on the lower reaches of the river, because there had been moldy rain of two to three inches in various inland areas, people's hearts were down and the appetite for all goods was lonely. The market price of white japonica rice fell by 20 to 30 cents, and early thin rice also fell by 20 cents. The other goods also fell by nearly 10 cents. However, the arrival and sale of white rice were both good, and the price situation was stable.

Foreign rice was originally in a gradual stage of recovery, but the heavy rain that penetrated everywhere the day before stabilized the minds of farmers in the interior. Yesterday, the inland area's sales were weak, and the market had a sharp downturn. However, the sales from Zhejiang were reduced, while the areas along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and Jiujiang and Hankou, as well as this street, all inquired about small quantities. Rain Not Thorough; Flour and Wheat Fall and Then Rise Again

Yesterday, the flour market saw a consistent decline in prices across all months. When prices opened, foreign wheat prices were reported to be low, and since all areas had received good rain after a long drought, people's hearts were naturally greatly comforted. Therefore, after prices opened, the market immediately saw a setback, falling about 3 points compared to the previous week's closing price. At that time, there was active short covering, while the factories' selling became increasingly strong. Jin Bang also bought near-term contracts, resulting in a stable trend in the following trading. When the market opened in the afternoon, transactions had cleared, and both sides were watching. Because the rain, although it had been seen, was still felt to be insufficient, the selling became average and the market showed a state of rejection. If the weather continues to be smooth in the future, then people's hearts will not easily be fixed. As a result, the price for this month fell 7.5 points, the price for July fell 3 points, the price for August fell 4 points, the price for September and October fell 2.7 points, and the price for November fell 1 point.

Yesterday, the wheat market saw a weak market for each month's market, with foreign wheat prices being quoted at 3 to 4 cents lower in Chicago and 8 cents to 1 point lower in Canada. After the market opened, the prices were dampened by the rain the day before. As people say, "a great drought meets the clouds," which greatly comforts people's hearts. The price for July immediately showed weakness, falling 5 to 6 points compared to the previous week. After that, both sides rejected each other and there were few people coming in and out. When the market opened in the afternoon, the flour market had not fallen sharply, and the inland areas were still dry. Therefore, the selling became sparse and people's hearts gradually recovered. However, after a long drought, the rain provided temporary peace of mind. As a result, the price for July fell 4 points, the price for August fell 6 points, and the price for September and October fell 5 points. The spot wheat market is still stable for high-quality goods, while medium-quality goods are lower by 2 to 3 points. It is said that wheat from Guandian, Linhuai Pass, and Mingguang is 3 yuan and 45 cents; wheat from Hankou Kunyou is 3 yuan and 26 cents; wheat from Chuzhou is 3 yuan and 42 cents; wheat from Shuangfeng is 3 yuan and 32 cents; wheat from Taiping is 3 yuan and 21 cents; wheat from Yangzhou is 2 yuan and 35 cents; wheat from Penglai is 3 yuan and 32 cents; wheat from Zhitang and Zhitang is 3 yuan and 33 cents; wheat from Wusong is 3 yuan and 31 cents; and wheat from Danyang Gaozi is 3 yuan and 27 cents. Unless the current extremely good harvest situation in overseas wheat markets changes, prices will eventually find it difficult to rise and not fall.
